ChinaRen校友录全新改版
四大产品构架中国最大的年轻人社区
2007年3月1日，全球华人最大的青年社区ChinaRen校友录正式改版上线，以橘色、绿色为主色调的新版ChinaRen校友录扑面而来的清新动感的气息，让所有网民眼前为之一亮。此次改版是2000年ChinaRen加入搜狐以来对校友录进行的第二次产品、版面、内容等方面的全面调整，改版后的ChinaRen校友录，不仅在页面结构、技术应用，板块内容和社区结合等方面大大提高用户的使用感受，它同“ChinaRen校内”、“ChinaRen社区”、“ChinaRen校园”等四大重量级产品共同构架的中国最大的年轻人社区，将Web2.0相关技术充分引入，将为在校以及离校的人们提供更人性化、更便捷的服务。
在刚刚过去的2006年ChinaRen先后进行过多次二级产品升级，体现在首页摒弃了table的页面结构，全站应用DIV+CSS的结构；大量的Ajax的应用，大大提高用户使用感受；板块内容和社区结合，自动更新最新精华贴和推荐贴等方面。由于在整个过程中出色地完成了对“年轻人的大社区”的理念实现，将Web2.0相关技术恰到好处地引入，并开发推出了新概念的重量级产品“ChinaRen校内”、“ChinaRen社区”、“ChinaRen校园”等，而备受业内人士关注以及用户好评。
作为ChinaRen的核心产品，“ChinaRen校友录”的全新改版可谓是四年磨一剑，对于用户而言，最直观的感受将会是校友录新版的年轻风格。此次改版主要包括：超大容量的班级相册，相册增容到100M，同时增加批量上传和超炫幻灯浏览的功能；新功能班级动态，可以第一时间了解新同学加入情况和同学的个人资料变化情况；增强的社区化功能，班级留言可以自定义字体和颜色，支持插入图片、音乐、视频；加强保护用户的隐私，用户可以设置个性资料的保密性；同时，新版校友录在搜狐矩阵的关联上也作出了新的尝试，如与搜狐博客进行互通，搜狐博客和校内日志的同学可以加入班级博客圈，展示自己的精彩博客生活。
经过八年的不断发展，ChinaRen的注册用户已超过1亿，页面日均访问量达到5000多万人次，其中最著名的校友录产品现有注册用户8000万，1000万个班级，日均访问量3000万人次，庞大的用户群和超高人气使其成为目前国内校友录产品的首选。ChinaRen校友录已经成为规模最大、数据最全、服务最稳定、发展最成功的校友录产品，影响遍及海内外。
2006年9月上线的
“ChinaRen校园”继承了其前身“搜狐校园频道”极高的人气以及品牌认知，结合校园论坛大力发展学生原创作品，一经上线就受到广大青年学生的喜爱；2005年1月上线的“ChinaRen社区”经过在两年多的发展，日均访问量突破2000万，创下了国内社区成长的奇迹；而2006年9月上线的“ChinaRen校内”是一个真实身份的校园社交网络，在这里用户可以建立自己的个性地盘，撰写大学生活日志，建立同学圈，和同学们一起讨论大学课程，业已成为网络人气最高的“大学生地盘”。改版后的“ChinaRen校友录”将和“ChinaRen校园”、“ChinaRen社区”、“ChinaRen校内”在内的四大重量级产品共同构架中国最大的年轻人社区。
搜狐公司董事局主席兼首席执行官张朝阳先生表示：“ChinaRen作为搜狐门户矩阵的重要成员，由最初的单一校友录，扩展到如今的ChinaRen社区、ChinaRen校内、ChinaRen校园，一直深受年轻网友的喜爱。此次针对校友录的改版，给用户带来的更直观的感受是校友录新版的年轻风格。我们会将‘年轻人的大社区’彻底贯彻到ChinaRen所有产品中去，为ChinaRen的领先市场地位提供更为坚实的保障，并对追赶竞争者形成壁垒”。
作为国内互联网市场的主流品牌之一，ChinaRen校友录在一如既往提供优质社区服务之余，是否会保持创新激情，不断自我超越，引领相关行业和技术向更高层面发展，为用户提供更多更好的应用体验，以及为互联网产业的社会化进步提供动力支持，这一切都非常值得观望，让我们拭目以待。

搜狐动态
2007
搜狐联手清华大学建立联合实验室
以搜索技术发展人工智能
2007年3月16日，搜狐公司与清华大学于搜狐网络大厦举行“清华大学（计算机系）-搜狐搜索技术联合实验室”的合作签字仪式和揭牌仪式。这是2008北京奥运会唯一互联网赞助商与中国顶尖研究型大学之间的“强强联合”，将为推进我国网络技术产业化以及服务2008北京奥运发挥重要的作用。
清华－搜狐搜索技术联合实验室的目标是让搜索更加智能化，同时以搜索技术带动人工智能的发展。由清华大学计算机系智能技术与系统国家重点实验室、软件研究所和搜狐研发中心共同建立，预计由60人组成，其中，清华大学35人，搜狐公司25人。目前，清华大学精挑细选的6名教师、15名学生，以及搜狐公司选派的10名技术人员已经到位，并且开始项目运作。
联合实验室将充分发挥清华大学在计算机科学领域的技术优势，结合搜狐公司的产品经验和市场优势，在网络信息检索领域研发基于自主知识产权的网络信息存储、检索、管理和应用技术，并且利用搜狐门户矩阵的平台，以及搜狐公司的数据、代码、经验等一线资源，快速完成技术向产品的转化，从而增强搜狐公司以网络信息服务为主的相关产品和服务核心竞争力，实现依靠科技创造未来的战略。
联合实验室设计了与以往全然不同的新的管理机制，简称为“双内循环机制”，形成双方水乳相融的决策和管理系统，设立管理委员会，以确定联合研究机构的研发目标和重大事务。管委会主任由搜狐副总裁王小川担任。实验室主任由清华大学计算机系教授、博士生导师马少平担任，副主任由双方各派一人担任。实验室主任负责执行管委会的决议，在管委会指导下主持研究开发项目和管理联合研究机构日常工作。
联合实验室的成果形式包括高水平学术论文以及相关技术发明专利。同时实验室也将积极参与国际重要评测（如TREC、TRECVID等）和国内相关评测，提高在国内外相关研究领域的影响力；并选定与行业技术发展密切相关的研究课题，更好地衔接高校人才培养和企业人才需求，在高水平合作研究中，促进尖端创新人才的成长。
清华大学副校长何建坤表示，与企业的联合研究机构是清华大学服务社会，为以企业为中心的国家技术创新体系做贡献的重要形式，作为国内领先的互联网企业，搜狐公司在互联网行业和互联网技术等方面的积累和资源等优势，将为清华大学的技术研发提供强有力的支持，清华大学非常看重与搜狐的合作，也非常确信清华-搜狐搜索技术联合实验室的研究成果对学校、企业、行业和社会产生有力的推动和深远的影响。
搜狐公司董事局主席兼首席执行官张朝阳表示，清华大学在计算机方面的基础研究领先国内，在世界范围内也有着明显的优势，搜狐公司拥有最有价值的网络门户矩阵以及数亿网民，双方的结合，必将对中国互联网行业的技术和整体发展，产生巨大的影响，搜狐公司也将在合作中受益，并将为网民提供更好的技术产品服务。回归中关村之后，搜狐一直致力于“技术驱动”和“产品导向”，为用户提供良好的互联网内容和服务体验，同清华大学的合作，将进一步强化搜狐的技术竞争优势，同时，清华的研发成果，通过搜狐可以迅速地转化成产品和服务，也将促进清华大学相关技术的研究。

Company
Profile
Sohu.com
Inc.
(NASDAQ: SOHU)
is
China's
premier
online
brand
and
indispensable
to
the
daily
life
of
millions
of
Chinese,
providing
a
network
of
web
properties
and
community
based/web
2.0
products
which
offer
the
vast
Sohu
user
community
a
broad
array
of
choices
regarding
information,
entertainment
and
communication.
Sohu
has
built
one
of
the
most
comprehensive
matrices
of
Chinese
language
web
properties
and
proprietary
search
engines,
consisting
of
seven
leading
web
properties.
more

News

HOME
Press
Room
2007
SOHU.COM
Announces
Key
Programs
In
Conjunction
With
Official
Internet
Sponsorship
Of
Beijing
2008
Olympic
Games
BEIJING,
CHINA,
March
26,
2007
C
Sohu.com
Inc.
(NASDAQ: SOHU),
China's
leading
online
media,
search
and
mobile
value-added
services
company,
today
announced
media
collaboration
and
other
key
programs
in
conjunction
with
Sohu’s
role
as
the
Official
Internet
Sponsor
of
the
Beijing
2008
Olympic
Games.
Ms.
Carol
Yu,
Co-President
and
CFO
of
Sohu,
stated,
“With
the
500-day
countdown
to
the
Beijing
2008
Olympic
Games,
athletes
and
sponsors
alike
are
preparing
for
the
first
Olympic
Games
to
be
held
in
China.
As
the
first
Internet
Content
Sponsor
in
the
history
of
the
Olympics,
Sohu
is
already
powering
the
official
Beijing
Olympics
website.
We
have
also
begun
implementing
more
than
20
key
programs,
together
with
the
Beijing
Organizing
Committee
for
the
Games
of
the
XXIX
Olympiad
(BOCOG),
to
highlight
enthusiasm
and
support
for
China’s
first
time
as
host
of
the
Olympic
Games.
These
programs
are
designed
to
attract
a
broad
range
of
Chinese
Internet
users
including
world-famous
athletes
and
Olympic
fans
alike.”
Leveraging
Sohu’s
unique
status
of
sole
Internet
Sponsor
and
operator
of
the
official
website
of
the
Beijing
2008
Olympic
Games,
Sohu
is
the
only
Chinese
online
media
company
to
have
exclusive
access
to
premier
Olympic
content.
As
such,
Sohu
is
announcing
an
exclusive
collaborative
agreement
with
the
nation’s
top
15
newspapers
in
setting
up
a
media
alliance
for
the
Beijing
2008
Olympic
Games.
The
members
of
the
alliance
will
join
Sohu’s
journalist
team
and
share
their
resources
to
provide
extensive
Olympics-related
coverage
and
reporting.
In
addition,
each
member
will
commit
to
promote
Sohu’s
unique
status
and
strengths
surrounding
the
Beijing
2008
Olympic
Games.
Mr.
Luming
Chen,
Vice
President
of
Olympic
Sponsorship
for
Sohu,
commented,
“Sohu’s
collaborative
agreement
with
China’s
leading
traditional
media
outlets
marks
the
first
time
multiple
media
outlets
are
working
together
to
report
on
the
Beijing
2008
Olympic
Games
in
a
format
that
underscores
the
importance
of
reaching
the
vast
Chinese
audience
through
both
traditional
and
new
media.”
In
addition
to
its
collaborative
media
program,
Sohu
also
announced
its
involvement
in
new
initiatives
and
programs
promoting
the
Beijing
2008
Olympic
Games
including:
-
Olympics
Families
Selection
C
A
Sohu-driven
initiative,
presented
on
the
Official
Olympic
website
(http://en.beijing2008.cn/),
to
select
and
invite
five
families
from
across
the
globe
and
five
families
from
China
to
attend
the
Beijing
2008
Olympic
Games
and
share
their
experiences.
-
International
Volunteers
Recruitment
C
A
program
to
raise
awareness
and
enrollment
for
volunteers
from
around
the
world
to
assist
with
the
administration
of
the
Beijing
2008
Olympic
Games.
-
Honorary
Website
Visitors
Selection
C
The
official
website
of
the
Beijing
2008
Olympic
Games
is
enrolling
a
total
of
2008
Honorary
Official
Website
Visitors
as
part
of
a
campaign
to
mark
the
500-day
countdown
to
the
Olympics.
On
March
26,
the
Official
Olympic
website
published
the
first
batch
of
500
Honorary
Visitors,
including
official
website
users,
BOCOG
officials,
sports
and
art
stars
(including world-famous female Chinese volleyball player Lang Ping),
volunteers,
and
people
with
disabilities.
The
Honorary
Visitors
will
take
part
in
special
activities
and
will
serve
as
"Online
Messengers"
of
the
Official
Website
of
the
Beijing
2008
Olympic
Games.
-
"Good
Luck
Beijing"
events
C
Test
games
for
Olympics
venues
which
will
occur
from
July
2007
to
June
2008.
The
events
will
include
42
games
featuring
global
competitors
from
28
Olympic
sports
and
two
Paralympic
sports.
Sohu
will
provide
timely
and
comprehensive
coverage
of
the
Good
Luck
Beijing
events
including
news
reporting,
coverage
on
Sohu
Blog
and
Sohu
Club,
video
highlights
and
video
interviews
with
the
athletes.
Dr.
Charles
Zhang,
Chairman
and
CEO
of
Sohu,
stated,
“The
Olympics
Games
are
not
only
the
world’s
premier
athletic
competition,
but
also
a
global
economic
and
cultural
event.
The
Olympics
offer
significant
opportunities
to
Beijing
as
well
as
cities
throughout
China.
Sohu,
as
the
sole
Internet
Sponsor,
is
devoted
to
providing
the
best
online
reporting
for
the
Beijing
2008
Olympics
and
encouraging
participation,
contribution
and
enjoyment
of
this
historic
event.”
Safe
Harbor
Statement
Statements
that
are
not
historical
facts,
including
statements
about
our
beliefs
and
expectations,
are
forward-looking
statements.
These
statements
are
based
on
current
plans,
estimates
and
projections,
and
therefore
you
should
not
place
undue
reliance
on
them.
Forward-looking
statements
involve
inherent
risks
and
uncertainties.
We
caution
you
that
a
number
of
important
factors
could
cause
actual
results
to
differ
materially
from
those
contained
in
any
forward-looking
statement.
Potential
risks
and
uncertainties
include,
but
are
not
limited
to,
the
uncertain
regulatory
landscape
in
the
People's
Republic
of
China,
fluctuations
in
Sohu’s
quarterly
operating
results,
Sohu's
historical
and
possible
future
losses
and
limited
operating
history,
and
the
company's
reliance
on
online
advertising
sales,
wireless
services
(most wireless revenues are collected from a few mobile network operators),
and
online
games
for
its
revenues.
Further
information
regarding
these
and
other
risks
is
included
in
Sohu's
annual
report
on
Form
10-K
for
the
year
ended
December
31,
2006,
and
other
filings
with
the
Securities
and
Exchange
Commission.
About
Sohu.com
Sohu.com
Inc.
(NASDAQ: SOHU)
is
China's
premier
online
brand
and
indispensable
to
the
daily
life
of
millions
of
Chinese,
providing
a
network
of
web
properties
and
community
based/web
2.0
products
which
offer
the
vast
Sohu
user
community
a
broad
array
of
choices
regarding
information,
entertainment
and
communication.
Sohu
has
built
one
of
the
most
comprehensive
matrices
of
Chinese
language
web
properties
and
proprietary
search
engines,
consisting
of
the
mass
portal
and
leading
online
media
destination
www.sohu.com;
interactive
search
engine
www.sogou.com;
#1
online
alumni
club
www.chinaren.com;
#1
games
information
portal
www.17173.com;
the
top
real
estate
website
www.focus.cn;
wireless
value-added
services
provider
www.goodfeel.com.cn;
and
leading
online
mapping
service
provider
www.go2map.com.
Sohu
corporate
services
consist
of
brand
advertising
on
its
matrix
of
websites
as
well
as
paid
listing
and
bid
listing
on
its
in-house
developed
search
directory
and
engines.
Sohu
also
offers
two
types
of
consumer
services.
Sohu
offers
wireless
value-added
services
such
as
news,
information,
music,
ringtone
and
picture
content
sent
over
mobile
phones.
The
company
also
operates
a
massively
multi-player
online
role-playing
game
and
a
casual
game
platform.
Sohu.com,
established
by
Dr.
Charles
Zhang,
one
of
China's
Internet
pioneers,
is
in
its
eleventh
year
of
operation.
Sohu.com

Information

Zhang
Senior
Manager

HOME
Press

2007
SOHU.COM
Announces
Appointment
Of
New
Board
And
Audit
Committee
Member
BEIJING,
CHINA,
April
16,
2007
C
Sohu.com
Inc.
(NASDAQ: SOHU),
China's
leading
online
media,
search
and
mobile
value-added
services
company,
today
announced
the
appointment
of
John
Deng,
Ph.D.
to
its
Board
of
Directors
and
audit
committee,
effective
immediately.
Dr.
Charles
Zhang,
Chairman
and
Chief
Executive
Officer
of
Sohu,
stated,
“We
are
delighted
to
welcome
Dr.
John
Deng
to
our
Board
of
Directors
and
audit
committee.
Dr.
Deng
is
recognized
internationally
as
a
premier
business
leader
in
China
and
a
catalyst
behind
creative
design
throughout
our
country.
His
perspectives
on
technological
trends
and
business
innovation
will
be
invaluable
for
Sohu
as
we
continue
to
drive
leading
developments
in
China’s
Internet
space.”
Dr.
John
Deng
is
the
Chairman
and
Chief
Executive
Officer
of
Vimicro
Corporation
(NASDAQ: VIMC),
a
leading
Chinese
semiconductor
design
company.
He
has
received
numerous
prestigious
awards
and
accolades
in
both
China
and
the
U.S.
for
his
achievements
in
developing
China's
personal
computer
industry.
These
include
three
Chinese
national
medals
and
China’s
National
First
Class
Award
for
Science
and
Technology
in
2005,
which
were
presented
by
Chinese
President
Hu
Jintao.
In
2005,
he
was
selected
by
China
Central
Television
(CCTV)
as
China's
Man
of
the
Year
and
received
a
Distinguished
Engineering
Alumni
Award
from
the
University
of
California
at
Berkeley,
College
of
Engineering.
In
September
2006,
Dr.
Deng
received
the
honor
of
presenting
alongside
Chinese
Premier
Wen
Jiabao
as
the
main
representative
of
Chinese
business
enterprises.
Dr.
Deng
received
a
Ph.D.
in
Electrical
Engineering
and
Computer
Sciences,
a
M.S.
degree
in
Economics
and
a
M.S.
degree
in
Physics,
all
from
the
University
of
California,
Berkeley.
Safe
Harbor
Statement
Statements
that
are
not
historical
facts,
including
statements
about
our
beliefs
and
expectations,
are
forward-looking
statements.
These
statements
are
based
on
current
plans,
estimates
and
projections,
and
therefore
you
should
not
place
undue
reliance
on
them.
Forward-looking
statements
involve
inherent
risks
and
uncertainties.
We
caution
you
that
a
number
of
important
factors
could
cause
actual
results
to
differ
materially
from
those
contained
in
any
forward-looking
statement.
Potential
risks
and
uncertainties
include,
but
are
not
limited
to,
the
uncertain
regulatory
landscape
in
the
People's
Republic
of
China,
fluctuations
in
Sohu’s
quarterly
operating
results,
Sohu's
historical
and
possible
future
losses
and
limited
operating
history,
and
the
company's
reliance
on
online
advertising
sales,
wireless
services
(most wireless revenues are collected from a few mobile network operators),
and
online
games
for
its
revenues.
Further
information
regarding
these
and
other
risks
is
included
in
Sohu's
annual
report
on
Form
10-K
for
the
year
ended
December
31,
2006,
and
other
filings
with
the
Securities
and
Exchange
Commission.
About
Sohu.com
Sohu.com
Inc.
(NASDAQ: SOHU)
is
China's
premier
online
brand
and
indispensable
to
the
daily
life
of
millions
of
Chinese,
providing
a
network
of
web
properties
and
community
based/web
2.0
products
which
offer
the
vast
Sohu
user
community
a
broad
array
of
choices
regarding
information,
entertainment
and
communication.
Sohu
has
built
one
of
the
most
comprehensive
matrices
of
Chinese
language
web
properties
and
proprietary
search
engines,
consisting
of
the
mass
portal
and
leading
online
media
destination
www.sohu.com;
interactive
search
engine
www.sogou.com;
#1
online
alumni
club
www.chinaren.com;
#1
games
information
portal
www.17173.com;
the
top
real
estate
website
www.focus.cn;
wireless
value-added
services
provider
www.goodfeel.com.cn;
and
leading
online
mapping
service
provider
www.go2map.com.
Sohu
corporate
services
consist
of
brand
advertising
on
its
matrix
of
websites
as
well
as
paid
listing
and
bid
listing
on
its
in-house
developed
search
directory
and
engines.
Sohu
also
offers
two
types
of
consumer
services.
Sohu
offers
wireless
value-added
services
such
as
news,
information,
music,
ringtone
and
picture
content
sent
over
mobile
phones.
The
company
also
operates
a
massive
multi-player
online
role-playing
game
and
a
casual
game
platform.
Sohu.com,
established
by
Dr.
Charles
Zhang,
one
of
China's
Internet
pioneers,
is
in
its
eleventh
year
of
operation.

To

1
BEIJING,
CHINA,
April
23,
2007
-
Sohu.com
Inc.
(NASDAQ: SOHU),
China's
leading
online
media,
communications,
search
and
mobile
value-added
services
company,
will
report
its
first
quarter
2007
unaudited
results
on
Tuesday,
May
1,
2007
after
U.S.
market
hours,
corresponding
with
Wednesday
morning,
May
2,
2007
Beijing/Hong
Kong
time.
Sohu's
management
team
will
host
a
conference
call
on
the
same
day
at
8:00
PM
EST,
May
1,
2007
(or 8:00 AM, May 2, 2007 Beijing/Hong Kong time)
following
the
quarterly
results
announcement.
To
listen
to
the
conference
call,
please
use
the
dial
in
numbers
below:
USA
Toll
Number:
1-800-238-9007
International:
1-719-457-2622
A
replay
of
the
call
will
be
available
for
two
weeks
following
the
call
and
can
be
accessed
by
dialing
the
numbers
below:
USA
Toll
Number:
1-888-203-1112
International:
1-719-457-0820
PASSCODE:
4638181
The
conference
call
will
be
available
on
webcast
live
and
available
for
replay
at:
About
Sohu.com
Sohu.com
Inc.
(NASDAQ: SOHU)
is
China's
premier
online
brand
and
indispensable
to
the
daily
life
of
millions
of
Chinese,
providing
a
network
of
web
properties
and
community
based/web
2.0
products
which
offer
the
vast
Sohu
user
community
a
broad
array
of
choices
regarding
information,
entertainment
and
communication.
Sohu
has
built
one
of
the
most
comprehensive
matrices
of
Chinese
language
web
properties
and
proprietary
search
engines,
consisting
of
the
mass
portal
and
leading
online
media
destination
www.sohu.com;
interactive
search
engine
www.sogou.com;
#1
online
alumni
club
www.chinaren.com;
#1
games
information
portal
www.17173.com;
the
top
real
estate
website
www.focus.cn;
wireless
value-added
services
provider
www.goodfeel.com.cn;
and
leading
online
mapping
service
provider
www.go2map.com.
Sohu
corporate
services
consist
of
brand
advertising
on
its
matrix
of
websites
as
well
as
paid
listing
and
bid
listing
on
its
in-house
developed
search
directory
and
engines.
Sohu
also
offers
two
types
of
consumer
services.
Sohu
offers
wireless
value-added
services
such
as
news,
information,
music,
ringtone
and
picture
content
sent
over
mobile
phones.
The
company
also
operates
a
massively
multi-player
online
role-playing
game
and
a
casual
game
platform.
Sohu.com,
established
by
Dr.
Charles
Zhang,
one
of
China's
Internet
pioneers,
is
in
its
eleventh
year
of

IR
HOME
Press
Room
2007
SOHU.COM
Reports
First
Quarter
2007
Unaudited
Financial
Results
First
Quarter
Brand
Advertising
Revenues
Increase
41%
Year-on-Year
to
Record
US$23.5
Million
BEIJING,
CHINA,
May
1,
2007
C
Sohu.com
Inc.
(NASDAQ: SOHU),
China's
leading
online
media,
search
and
mobile
value-added
services
company,
today
reported
unaudited
financial
results
for
the
first
quarter
ended
March
31,
2007.
First
Quarter
Highlights
・
Record
brand
advertising
revenues
of
US$23.5
million,
up
41%
year-on-year
and
7%
quarter-on-quarter,
exceeding
company
guidance.
・
Record
advertising
revenues
of
US$25.6
million,
up
27%
year-on-year
and
3%
quarter-on-quarter,
meeting
company
guidance.
・
Non-advertising
revenue
of
US$7.5
million,
down
27%
year-on-year
and
21%
quarter-on-quarter,
meeting
company
guidance.
・
Total
revenues
of
US$33.1
million,
up
9%
year-on-year
and
down
4%
quarter-on-quarter,
meeting
company
guidance.
・
Non-GAAP
net
income
(i.e. excluding share-based compensation expenses)
of
US$7.0
million
or
US$0.18
per
fully
diluted
share,
meeting
company
guidance.
・
GAAP
net
income
of
US$4.5
million
or
US$0.12
per
fully
diluted
share.
・
Sohu
made
significant
progress
on
the
integration
of
Sohu
products
and
registration
systems
by
implementing
“Sohu
Passport”,
a
new
service
that
facilitates
complete
integration
of
all
Sohu
web
properties
and
seamless
surfing
of
most
products
within
the
Sohu
family
under
a
single
user
profile.
・
On
April
4,
2007,
Sohu’s
in-house
developed
massive
multiplayer
online
role-playing
game,
Tian
Long
Ba
Bu
(TLBB),
entered
into
final
closed
beta
testing
with
initial
success.
TLBB
will
start
its
open
beta
testing
on
May
9,
2007.
・
Explanation
of
the
Company’s
non-GAAP
financial
measures
and
the
related
reconciliations
to
GAAP
financial
measures
are
included
in
the
accompanying
“Non-GAAP
Disclosure”
and
the
“Reconciliation
to
Unaudited
Condensed
Consolidated
Statements
of
Operations.”
Dr.
Charles
Zhang,
Chairman
and
CEO
of
Sohu,
commented,
“We
are
continuing
to
build
on
Sohu’s
core
strengths
with
another
quarter
of
record
brand
advertising
revenue.
This
clearly
reflects
advertisers’
recognition
of
Sohu’s
premier
content
and
the
continued
expanded
user-base
brought
by
our
innovation
and
product
enhancements,
and
the
increasing
Sohu
branding
associated
with
the
approach
of
the
Beijing
2008
Olympic
Games.
For
the
rest
of
2007,
our
catalysts
for
brand
advertising
and
online
games
are
strong
near-term
positives.
For
the
longer-term,
we
continue
to
devote
our
efforts
to
develop
our
technology,
which
we
believe
has
not
only
enhanced
our
own
business
but
has
created
an
opportunity
for
us
to
continue
to
be
a
thought
leader
in
the
way
new
technologies
change
the
Internet
industry
in
China.”
First
Quarter
Financial
Results
Total
revenues
for
first
quarter
ended
March
31,
2007
totaled
US$33.1
million,
compared
to
revenues
of
US$34.4
million
for
fourth
quarter
ended
December
31,
2006,
and
US$30.4
million
for
first
quarter
ended
March
31,
2006.
Gross
margin
of
61%
in
first
quarter
of
2007
decreased
from
63%
in
the
previous
quarter
and
67%
in
the
same
period
of
2006.
Non-GAAP
gross
margin
was
62%
in
the
first
quarter
of
2007,
down
from
65%
in
the
previous
quarter
and
68%
in
the
same
period
of
2006.
Net
income
for
first
quarter
of
2007
was
US$4.5
million
or
US$0.12
per
fully
diluted
share.
Non-GAAP
net
income
for
first
quarter
of
2007
was
US$7.0
million
or
US$0.18
per
fully
diluted
share.
This
compares
to
non-GAAP
net
income
of
US$8.1
million
or
US$0.21
per
fully
diluted
share
for
fourth
quarter
2006
and
US$7.8
million
or
US$0.20
per
fully
diluted
share
for
first
quarter
of
2006.
Advertising
revenues
for
first
quarter
of
2007
totaled
US$25.6
million,
a
27%
year-on-year
increase
and
a
3%
quarter-on-quarter
increase.
Advertising
revenues,
consisting
of
US$23.5
million
in
brand
advertising
and
US$2.1
million
in
sponsored
search,
accounted
for
77%
of
total
revenues
in
the
first
quarter
of
2007.
Brand
advertising
revenues
for
first
quarter
of
2007
increased
7%
quarter-on-quarter
and
41%
year-on-year.
Sponsored
search
revenues
for
first
quarter
of
2007
decreased
29%
quarter-on
quarter
and
40%
year-on-year.
Advertising
gross
margin
for
first
quarter
of
2007
was
62%,
down
from
65%
in
the
previous
quarter
and
73%
in
the
first
quarter
of
2006.
Non-GAAP
advertising
gross
margin
for
first
quarter
of
2007
was
64%,
down
from
66%
in
the
previous
quarter
and
75%
in
the
first
quarter
of
2006.
The
declines
in
gross
margin
were
primarily
due
to
the
increase
in
content
costs,
bandwidth
and
server
depreciation
costs.
For
the
first
quarter
of
2007,
Sohu's
non-advertising
revenues,
which
are
derived
mainly
from
wireless
value-added
services
and
online
games,
were
US$7.5
million,
representing
23%
of
total
revenues.
Non-advertising
gross
margin
was
56%
compared
to
60%
in
the
previous
quarter
and
55%
in
first
quarter
of
2006.
Non-GAAP
non-advertising
gross
margin
was
56%
compared
to
60%
in
the
previous
quarter
and
55%
in
the
first
quarter
of
2006.
The
decline
in
non-advertising
gross
margin
was
primarily
due
to
the
decreased
mix
of
higher
margin
revenues,
a
decrease
in
gross
margin
of
certain
wireless
products
and
the
increased
server
depreciation
costs
for
our
existing
game.
For
first
quarter
of
2007,
Sohu's
operating
expenses
totaled
US$16.0
million.
Non-GAAP
operating
expenses
totaled
US$13.9
million,
a
decrease
of
4%
from
the
previous
quarter
and
up
9%
year-on-year.
The
quarter-on-quarter
decrease
was
mainly
due
to
the
decrease
of
our
marketing
expenses,
while
the
year-on-year
increase
was
primarily
due
to
our
increased
re-investment
in
R&amp;D
for
technology
projects
and
product
development,
and
increased
marketing
expenses
for
branding.
As
of
March
31,
2007,
Sohu's
balance
of
cash,
cash
equivalents
and
investments
in
marketable
debt
securities
was
US$97.5
million,
compared
to
US$129.7
million
and
US$137.5
million
as
of
December
31,
2006
and
March
31,
2006,
respectively.
The
reduction
in
cash,
cash
equivalents
and
investments
in
marketable
debt
securities
was
due
to
the
company’s
purchase
of
its
Beijing
headquarters
at
a
purchase
price
of
approximately
$35.3
million,
in
January
2007.
Ms.
Carol
Yu,
Co-president
and
CFO
of
Sohu.com,
stated,
“We
are
pleased
with
the
financial
results
we
achieved
in
the
first
quarter
of
2007.
Although
it
was
a
seasonally
weak
quarter,
our
brand
advertising
revenue
reached
a
historical
record
and
exceeded
our
guidance.
Our
investments
in
premium
video
content,
corporate
branding
and
new
products
have
started
to
pay
off.
With
the
increasing
momentum
from
the
rapidly
approaching
Beijing
2008
Olympics
Games
and
our
new
online
game
TLBB,
which
will
be
contributing
to
our
results
in
the
second
half
of
2007,
we
are
well
positioned
to
have
a
good
year.”
Business
Outlook
Sohu
estimates
total
revenues
for
the
second
quarter
of
2007
to
be
between
US$35.5
million
to
US$37.5
million,
with
advertising
revenues
of
US$26.5
million
to
US$27.5
million
and
non-advertising
revenues
of
US$9
million
to
US$10
million.
Sohu
estimates
brand
advertising
revenues
for
the
second
quarter
of
2007
to
be
between
US$24.5
million
to
US$25.0
million.
Sohu
expects
to
invest
approximately
$1
million
for
server
depreciation
costs,
bandwidth
and
marketing
of
our
new
online
game,
TLBB,
for
the
second
quarter
of
2007.
Sohu
estimates
non-GAAP
fully
diluted
earnings
per
share
for
the
second
quarter
of
2007
to
be
between
US$0.17
and
US$0.19.
Assuming
no
new
grants
of
share-based
awards,
Sohu
estimates
share-based
compensation
expense
for
the
second
quarter
of
2007
to
be
between
US$2.3
million
and
US$2.4
million.
The
estimated
impact
of
this
expense
is
expected
to
reduce
Sohu's
fully
diluted
earnings
per
share
for
the
second
quarter
of
2007,
under
US
GAAP,
by
US$0.06.
Non-GAAP
Disclosure
To
supplement
the
unaudited
consolidated
financial
statements
presented
in
accordance
with
United
States
Generally
Accepted
Accounting
Principles
(“GAAP”),
Sohu’s
management
uses
non-GAAP
measures
of
cost
of
revenues,
operating
expenses,
net
income
and
net
income
per
share,
which
are
adjusted
from
results
based
on
GAAP
to
exclude
the
compensation
cost
of
share-based
awards
granted
to
employees
under
Statement
of
Financial
Accounting
Standard
123R,
effective
from
January
1,
2006.
These
measures
should
be
considered
in
addition
to
results
prepared
in
accordance
with
GAAP,
but
should
not
be
considered
a
substitute
for,
or
superior
to,
GAAP
results.
Sohu’s
management
believes
excluding
the
share-based
compensation
expense
from
its
non-GAAP
financial
measure
is
useful
for
itself
and
investors.
Further,
the
amount
of
share-based
compensation
expense
cannot
be
anticipated
by
management
and
business
line
leaders
and
these
expenses
were
not
built
into
the
annual
budgets
and
quarterly
forecasts,
which
have
been
the
basis
for
information
Sohu
provides
to
analysts
and
investors
as
guidance
for
future
operating
performance.
As
share-based
compensation
expense
does
not
involve
any
upfront
or
subsequent
cash
outflow,
Sohu
does
not
factor
this
in
when
evaluating
and
approving
expenditures
or
when
determining
the
allocation
of
its
resources
to
its
business
segments.
As
a
result,
the
monthly
financial
results
for
internal
reporting
and
any
performance
measure
for
commission
and
bonus
are
based
on
non-GAAP
financial
measures
that
exclude
share-based
compensation
expense.
The
non-GAAP
financial
measures
are
provided
to
enhance
the
investors’
overall
understanding
of
Sohu’s
current
financial
performance
and
prospects
for
the
future.
A
limitation
of
using
non-GAAP
cost
of
revenues,
operating
expenses,
net
income
and
net
income
per
share,
excluding
share-based
compensation
expenses
is
that
the
share-based
compensation
charge
has
been
and
will
continue
to
be
a
significant
recurring
expense
in
our
business
for
the
foreseeable
future.
In
order
to
mitigate
these
limitations
we
have
provided
specific
information
regarding
the
GAAP
amounts
excluded
from
each
non-GAAP
measure.
The
accompanying
tables
include
details
on
the
reconciliation
between
GAAP
financial
measures
that
are
most
directly
comparable
to
the
non-GAAP
financial
measures
we
have
presented.
Notes
to
Financial
Information
Financial
information
in
this
press
release
other
than
the
information
indicated
as
being
non-GAAP
is
extracted
from
Sohu's
unaudited
financial
statements
prepared
in
accordance
with
generally
accepted
accounting
principles
in
the
United
States.
On
June
20,
2006,
Sohu
discontinued
its
own
e-commerce
platform
of
physical
consumer
goods.
While
processing
the
disposal
of
its
e-commerce
business,
Sohu
is
reporting
the
related
business
activities
as
discontinued
operations.
Sohu’s
income
statement
separates
out
discontinued
operations
for
both
current
and
prior
periods
in
order
to
focus
on
continuing
operations
and
provide
a
consistent
basis
for
comparing
financial
performance
over
time.

Statement

contains

statements.
It

for

reason.
Statements
that
are
not

about

forward-looking
statements.
These

are
based
on
current

estimates
and
projections,
and
therefore
you
should
not
place
undue
reliance
on

Forward-looking
statements
involve
inherent
risks
and
uncertainties.
We

you
that
a
number
of
important
factors
could
cause

results
to

from

in

in

About
Sohu.com
Sohu.com
Inc.
(NASDAQ: SOHU)
is
China's
premier
online
brand
and
indispensable
to
the
daily
life
of
millions
of
Chinese,
providing
a
network
of
web
properties
and
community
based/web
2.0
products
which
offer
the
vast
Sohu
user
community
a
broad
array
of
choices
regarding
information,
entertainment
and
communication.
Sohu
has
built
one
of
the
most
comprehensive
matrices
of
Chinese
language
web
properties
and
proprietary
search
engines,
consisting
of
the
mass
portal
and
leading
online
media
destination
www.sohu.com;
interactive
search
engine
www.sogou.com;
#1
online
alumni
club
www.chinaren.com;
#1
games
information
portal
www.17173.com;
the
top
real
estate
website
www.focus.cn;
wireless
value-added
services
provider
www.goodfeel.com.cn;
and
leading
online
mapping
service
provider
www.go2map.com.
Sohu
corporate
services
consist
of
brand
advertising
on
its
matrix
of
websites
as
well
as
paid
listing
and
bid
listing
on
its
in-house
developed
search
directory
and
engines.
Sohu
also
offers
two
types
of
consumer
services.
Sohu
offers
wireless
value-added
services
such
as
news,
information,
music,
ringtone
and
picture
content
sent
over
mobile
phones.
The
company
also
operates
a
massively
multi-player
online
role-playing
game
and
a
casual
game
platform.
Sohu.com,
established
by
Dr.
Charles
Zhang,
one
of
China's
Internet
pioneers,
is
in
its
eleventh
year
of
operation.

搜狐公司
搜狐动态
2007
搜狐公司公布2007年第一季度未经审计财务报告
2007年第一季度品牌广告收入达到创记录的2350万美元，比上年同期增长41%
中国北京，2007年5月1日
C
搜狐
(Nasdaq: SOHU)，中国领先的互联网媒体、搜索及移动增值服务公司，今天公布了未经审计的、截至2007年3月31日的2007年第一季度财务报告。
2007年第一季度重要业绩
-
品牌广告收入达到创记录的2350万美元，比去年同期增长41%，比上一季度增长7%，高于公司预期
-
广告收入达到创记录的2560万美元，比去年同期增长27%，比上一季度增长3%，达到公司预期
-
非广告收入750万美元，比去年同期下降27%，比上一季度下降21%，达到公司预期
-
总收入3310万美元，比去年同期增长9%，比上一季度下降4%，达到公司预期
-
非美国通用会计准则净利润（即不包括股票激励的费用）为700万美元，即每股摊薄净收益18美分，达到公司预期
-
美国通用会计准则净利润450万美元，即每股摊薄净收益12美分
-通过“搜狐通行证”的上线，搜狐在整合旗下产品和注册系统方面取得了重大进展。搜狐通行证是一项新的服务，它帮助打通了搜狐门户矩阵，实现了一证通行搜狐的畅游梦想。
-
2007年4月4日，搜狐自主研发的多角色扮演在线游戏“天龙八部”进入终极内测阶段，并取得初步成功。“天龙八部”将于2007年5月9日进入公测阶段
-
关于公司非美国通用会计准则财务数据以及对应美国通用会计准则财务数据所做的相关调整的说明参见“非美国通用会计准则披露”的附注和“对未经审计的简要合并损益表调整表”
搜狐公司董事会主席兼首席执行官张朝阳先生说：“我们不断提高搜狐的核心竞争力，并取得了又一季度创记录的品牌广告收入。这清楚地表明广告客户对搜狐的领先内容、创新和产品所带来的持续扩大的用户基础、以及成为2008北京奥运会赞助商所带来的品牌提升的认可。2007年，我们的品牌广告和在线游戏将带来强有力的近期优势。而长期来看，我们将持续致力于技术进步，这不仅将加强我们商业上的成功，还将在技术改变中国互联网行业的道路上，使我们持续成为富有远见的领导者。”
2007年第一季度财务业绩
截至2007年3月31日的2007年第一季度总收入为3310万美元，较之于截至2006年12月31日的2006年第四季度总收入为3440万美元，与截至2006年3月31日的2006年第一季度的总收入为3040万美元。
2007年第一季度的毛利率为61%，低于上季度的63%和2006年同期的67%。2007年第一季度的非美国通用会计准则毛利率为62%，低于上一季度的65%和2006年同期的68%。
2007年第一季度的净利润为450万美元，即每股摊薄净收益12美分。2007年第一季度的非美国通用会计准则净利润为700万美元，即每股摊薄净收益18美分，较之于2006年第四季度的非美国通用会计准则净利润810万美元，即每股摊薄净收益21美分，与2006年第一季度的净利润780万美元，即每股摊薄净收益20美分。
2007年第一季度的广告收入为2560万美元，比去年同期增长27%，比上一季度增长3%。广告收入包括2350万美元的品牌广告收入和210万美元的付费搜索收入，共构成2007年第一季度总收入的77%。2007年第一季度的品牌广告收入比上季度增加7%，比去年同期增加41%。2007年度第一季度的付费搜索收入比上季度下降29%，比去年同期下降40%。2007年第一季度广告业务的毛利率为62%，低于上季度的65%和2006年第一季度的73%。2007年第一季度广告业务的非美国通用会计准则毛利率为64%，低于上季度的66%和2006年第一季度的75%。毛利率的下降主要是由于内容成本、带宽成本和服务器折旧成本的上升。
2007年第一季度，搜狐公司的非广告收入为750万美元，占总收入的23%，主要来自无线增值服务和在线游戏。非广告收入毛利率为56%，较之于上一季度的60％，与2006年第一季度为55%。非广告收入的非美国通用会计准则毛利率为56%，较之于上一季度的60％，与2006年第一季度的55%。非广告业务毛利率下降主要是由于较高毛利率产品比重的下降，部分无线产品毛利率的下降，以及我们现有在线游戏的服务器折旧成本的上升。
2007年第一季度，搜狐公司的营业费用为1600万美元。非美国通用会计准则营业费用为1390万美元，比上一季度下降4%，比去年同期增长9%。营业费用与上一季度相比下降，主要是由于市场费用的减少，而与去年同期相比增长，主要是由于搜狐继续增加对研发的投入，以及市场费用的上升。
截止于2007年3月31日，搜狐公司的现金、现金等价物及可变现债券投资余额为9750万美元，较之于2006年12月31日的1亿2970万美元，和2006年3月31日的1亿3750万美元。
现金、现金等价物及可变现债券投资余额的下降主要是因为搜狐购买了北京总部的办公楼，购买价格约为3530万美元。
搜狐公司联席总裁和首席财务官余楚媛女士说，“我们对2007年第一季度所取得的财务业绩感到满意。尽管这是一个业务淡季，我们的品牌广告收入仍创历史新高，并超过了公司预期。我们在优质内容、视频内容、公司品牌和新产品上的投入开始取得回报。因2008北京奥运会的临近对品牌广告的推动，以及新游戏‘天龙八部’，将为2007年下半年的业绩做出贡献。我们已做好充分准备来迎接一个良好的年度。”
业务展望
搜狐公司预计2007年第二季度的总收入在3550万美元至3750万美元之间，其中广告收入为2650万美元至2750万美元之间，非广告收入为900万美元至1000万美元之间。搜狐公司预计2007年第二季度的品牌广告收入在2450万美元至2500万美元之间。
搜狐预计在2007年第二季度投入约100万美元，用于我们新的在线游戏“天龙八部”的服务器折旧、宽带以及市场费用。搜狐公司预计2007年第二季度的非美国通用会计准则每股摊薄净收益为17美分至19美分之间。
假设在不增发其他股票激励的情况下，搜狐预计2007年第二季度的股票激励的费用在230万美元至240万美元之间。该项费用预期将使搜狐公司2007年第二季度的美国通用会计准则每股摊薄净收益减少6美分。
非美国通用会计准则披露
作为对遵照美国通用会计准则提交的未经审计的合并财务报表的补充，搜狐公司管理层提供了非美国通用会计准则成本、经营费用、净利润和每股净收益，即将2006年1月1日起生效的SFAS123R规定股票激励的费用从美国通用会计准则数据中调整出。提供非美国通用会计准则财务数据旨在加强投资者对搜狐公司当前财务业绩和未来前景的总体理解。这些数据应被视为对遵照美国通用会计准则编制的财务报告的补充，而不应被视为可代替或优于美国通用会计准则数据。
搜狐公司管理层认为，不包括股票激励费用的非美国通用会计准则净收入对其本身和投资者都有其用处。并且，公司管理层和业务领导无法预计股票激励费用的金额，公司做年度预算和季度预测，即提供给投资者和分析师的业务展望的基础时也不考虑这部分费用。由于股票激励费用不涉及任何过去或将来的现金流，搜狐在评估和审批费用支出以及分配资源至各业务部门时都不会考虑此因素。因此，各月的内部财务报告和所有的绩效奖励考核都是基于不含股票激励费用的非美国通用会计准则进行的。
非美国通用会计准则财务数据帮助投资者了解搜狐目前的财务状况和对未来的展望。使用非美国通用会计准则的成本、经营费用、净利润和每股净收益也有其不足之处，股票激励费用已经是而且在可预见的将来也会是我们业务中一项重大持续费用。为了弥补这部分不足，我们同时提供了关于美国通用会计准则金额和非美国通用会计准则差别的具体信息。在后文的附表里列示了美国通用会计准则和非美国通用会计准则调整的明细，可以直观地进行比较。
财务报告附注
本财务报告中的财务信息（不包括非美国通用会计准则财务信息）是从按照美国通用会计准则准备的未经审计的搜狐公司财务报表中摘录的。
2006年6月20日起，搜狐公司终止运营其电子商务平台，并将相关业务视为终止经营业务。为了使读者更关注持续经营业务，并保持财务数据的一致性，搜狐公司本期和以前期间的损益表中将单独披露终止经营业务。
有关前瞻性陈述的警告声明
本财务报告中包含前瞻性的陈述。我们现在预期“业务展望”中的内容在下个季度财务报告公布之前不会被更新。但是，搜狐公司保留在任何时候，由于任何原因对“业务展望”部分的内容进行更新的权利。
非历史事实的陈述，包括关于我们的信念及预期的陈述，均为前瞻性陈述。这些陈述是基于当前的计划，估计及预期，请不要对其产生不适当的依赖。前瞻性的陈述中包含风险及不确定因素。我们提醒您一些重要的因素会导致实际结果与前瞻性陈述有重大差别。潜在的风险及不确定因素包括但不限于：中华人民共和国产业政策的不确定、各季度运营结果可能出现上下波动、搜狐公司过去及未来可能的亏损、有限的营业历史、以及本公司仰赖在线广告销售、无线业务（其收入主要通过数家移动电信运营商取得）和在线游戏作为主要收入来源的事实。更多有关上述及其他风险的资讯收录于截至2006年12月31日的搜狐公司年报和10-K表格，以及向美国证券交易委员会提交的其他文件中。

关于搜狐公司
搜狐公司
(NASDAQ: SOHU)是中国领先的互联网品牌，是中国人生活中不可缺少的一部分，搜狐的网络资产以及基于web2.0产品的社区给众多的SOHU用户在信息、娱乐、交流、商务领域提供了非常广泛的选择可能。SOHU建立了中国最全面的互联网资产组合之一和自有搜索引擎，其中包括最大的门户和中国领先的互联网媒体网站
www.sohu.com；互动搜索引擎www.sogou.com；中国第一在线校友录www.chinaren.com；中国第一网络游戏信息门户
www.17173.com；顶尖的房地产网站www.focus.cn；无线移动增值服务提供商
www.goodfeel.com.cn；以及领先的地图服务提供商www.go2map.com。
搜狐公司的企业客户服务包括在其网络矩阵上投放的在线广告以及在其自主研发的搜索引擎上投放的付费搜索和竞价搜索广告服务。搜狐公司还提供两种个人用户服务：包括基于手机的新闻、资讯、音乐、铃声和图片下载等无线增值服务，一款多角色扮演在线游戏和一个休闲游戏平台。SOHU.COM由中国互联网先驱张朝阳先生创办，已经成功运作十一年。

2007
搜狐3.0大厦全线落成亮相
顶级明星万名博客齐聚狂欢盛典
公元2007年7月21日，规模空前的搜狐第二届博客大会暨搜狐3.0落成大典在北京朝阳公园隆重启幕！各博客圈达人、名博、娱乐界明星和万名搜狐草根博客齐聚搜狐第二届博客大会，共同见证搜狐博客2007“声・色”版颠覆博客的表达方式、搜狐通行证实现一证畅游搜狐门户矩阵、以及Web2.0时代通讯工具“小纸条”等众多产品功能搭建的搜狐3.0正式落成。为庆祝互联网界空前盛事，林俊杰、羽泉、小柯、何洁、阿朵、黄圣依、叶蓓、瞿颖、胡灵、后舍男生、搜狗女声等众多演艺界大腕和网络达人倾情助阵，生动演绎“声色”俱佳的万人演唱会！藉此盛事向世人昭示着“搜狐3.0”时代的精彩到来！
搜狐
3.0
全线落成亮相
<?xml:namespace prefix = o ns = "urn:schemas-microsoft-com:office:office" />
“大本营”升起“搜狐<?xml:namespace prefix = st1 ns = "urn:schemas-microsoft-com:office:smarttags" />
3.0”
大旗
三年来以“技术驱动，产品导向”的重大成果――搜狐3.0全线落成，这是搜狐乃至中国互联网史上极具里程碑意义的标志性旗帜！由打造搜狐3.0全线服务的搜狐技术核心人员传递，并最终由搜狐3.0的缔造者
张朝阳
先生在万名博友见证下，在搜狐大本营升起了这面“搜狐
3.0”
大旗，至此拉开了第二届搜狐博客大会的序幕。
搜狐3.0是以博客为上网入口的个人门户，通过通行证整合搜狐矩阵所有产品，包括1.0和2.0的产品和内容，以及网络视频产品和搜狐博客2007“声・色”版，使搜狐矩阵用户能够通过小纸条随时随地沟通。搜狐3.0的落成，将搜狐门户矩阵内各网站的服务和用户全部整合，使用户可以轻松享受搜狐矩阵内的全部互联网内容和产品服务，搜狐用户体验将全面提升。
搜狐博客“声・色”版开启博客新时代
随着互联网技术的进步，搜狐博客的每一次革新更成为中国博客发展的风向标。在搜狐第二届博客大会上,搜狐博客2007“声・色”版闪亮登场。在2006“玩・弄”版的基础上全面升级的搜狐博客“声色”版，将全面支持视频内容的上传和分享。当博友们不再满足于“玩文字”、“弄图片”、“玩音乐”、“弄新闻”、“玩游戏”等搜狐博客的“玩・弄”乐趣之后，搜狐博客2007“声・色”版将为您带来缤纷动感的视频体验。震撼的电影片段，网络最新视频，动感体育集锦，自拍自导自演……在搜狐博客空间内尽情“玩弄”“声色”，将视频、音乐、图片、文字随意支配于掌股，打造最有个性的博客空间。
搜狐博客“声色”版不仅是搜狐3.0的集大成产品，汇聚了最顶尖的互联网技术和网络应用，更代表了中国博客未来的发展方向。自2006年搜狐首届博客大会推出其空间无限的图片公园、搜狗音乐盒的即时播放、随心定制的“玩”“弄”等个性化设置，让博友们充分享受“玩弄”博客的前卫观念后，2007搜狐博客“声色”版再掀博客界的新一轮技术革命，将人与人之间通过互联网交流互动的模式带到一个“绘声绘色”的新时代。
搜狐“通行证”让你一证畅游搜狐矩阵
搜狐3.0落成大典上，标志性产品之一的搜狐通行证让用户切身感受到其畅游搜狐门户矩阵的强大功能。只要用户拥有搜狐矩阵内搜狐、搜狗、CHINAREN、焦点、17173的任一帐号，即可登录搜狐博客、搜狐社区、CHINAREN校友录、CHINAREN校内、CHINAREN社区、搜狐邮箱、图片公园、搜狗说吧、搜狗音乐盒、焦点业主论坛、焦点装修论坛，17173游戏论坛、搜狐网络游戏等诸多搜狐产品，享受搜狐矩阵内各网站提供的所有互联网服务，真正实现一证通行搜狐矩阵的畅游梦想。并能充分享受为广大网友量身定制的各种网上个性化服务。
搜狐通行证不仅打通了搜狐门户矩阵，还有智能化记忆存储功能，搜狐用户的足迹将在搜狐通行证上留下“脚印”。用户不论到过门户矩阵中哪个网站，或是在哪个产品上逗留，搜狐通行证都将为用户完整的保留足迹，让搜狐用户在下次登录搜狐通行证的时候，能便捷的直接通过通行证的记录功能进入任何曾经去过的角落。搜狐通行证可谓是搜狐3.0时代网友在搜狐门户矩阵畅行无阻的贴身凭证，网民拥有搜狐通行证就拥有了搜狐门户矩阵的所有产品和服务。
小纸条点亮搜狐矩阵
博客大会现场的“寻找失落的博客”趣味活动中，一个传递小纸条的环节和任务让无数博友们津津乐道，仿佛时光倒流回到学生时同学间传递小纸条的那份纯真年代。小纸条是搜狐
3.0
的另一重大标志性产品。
随着搜狐3.0的到来，基于Web端的即时与延时通讯工具――搜狐小纸条将作为搜狐主线产品的联络工具，无需下载安装任何客户端或插件，只要用户拥有搜狐通行证，就能通过小纸条自由在线交流互动和离线留言。
小纸条伴随搜狐通行证轻松进驻搜狐矩阵内几乎所有重要产品，包括搜狐博客、搜狐社区、ChinaRen校内、ChinaRen校友录、ChinaRen社区、搜狗说吧、17173社区等，并统一覆盖了搜狐的好友系统。个性化的“蜡烛人”跟在用户昵称后，向其他用户显示了用户的在线/离线状态、用户的心情和性别等信息，也为添加好友和发送消息提供了入口。当收到新消息或有好友上线时，小纸条提示器将以右下角升起窗口的形式，为用户提供实时的提示服务。让用户第一时间收到好友讯息。搜狐小纸条的诞生不只是交流沟通的工具，还将成为一个资源共享、信息传递、关系传递等多元化、全方位的通讯工具，引领网民进入沟通交流的新境界。
第二届搜狐博客大会：博客群活动精彩纷呈
万人演唱会规模空前
“大本营”抢先体验搜狐3.0
“大本营”堪称搜狐3.0的坚定后方，搜狐大本营是作为用户登录搜狐博客后的私有页面出现，在这里，用户可以方便的进入搜狐门户矩阵的各个角落。搜狐大本营不仅是搜狐各个极具搜狐3.0特征产品的聚集地，搜狐博客大会将大本营从线上搬到线下，大本营是搜狐产品集中体验区，该区涉及到：博客声色版体验、搜狗输入法用户体验、搜狗音乐盒用户体验、搜狐社区版聊体验、CHINAREN校友录校园区体验、数码公社线下体验、说吧与贴吧线下体验、天龙八部cosplay等。通过网友集中体验与交流互动，切身感受搜狐3.0带来的技术震撼和个性化的用户体验。

大主题博客圈，通过奥运文化进校园
--MINI
奥运会、劲歌热舞足球赛、香车美女时装秀、疯狂英语、涂鸦、行为艺术、攀岩、短剧等等数十组主题活动和精彩无限的贴心礼品，使每个博客群成为草根博友与莫慧兰、李阳、高敏、王秋杨、张朝阳等名博牛人们畅谈游乐的据点。
4
大博客圈共同精心设置了主题为“寻找失落的博客”的趣味活动，参加活动的博友们通过博导手册详细了解活动的
10
大任务攻略并领取一块搜狐博客“声・色”版的模板框架，到
NPC
出现地点领取各博客模块贴纸做任务奖励，将博客模块贴纸对号贴入博客框架图内完成任务从而获得最终大奖。据悉，这项主题活动吸引了高达一千名博友参与其中，在“玩・弄”的乐趣中，了解搜狐博客“声・色”版各项功能的全新体验，感受搜狐博客“声・色”升级的无限精彩。
搜狐博客大会巧妙的将博客从线上搬到线下，精心设置的游戏环节，环环相扣，博友们在紧张与玩乐的氛围中彻底颠覆传统博客“舞文弄字”的概念，“通行证”让搜狐博友们畅游博客大会，“小纸条”让志同道合的博友把酒言欢，草根名博们在“大本营”尽情撒野，更具个性化和玩弄乐趣的搜狐博客“声・色”版改写博客历史，开创博客生活新纪元。
搜狐年度博客：刘翔
自搜狐首届博客大会评选出年度人物，草根文化成为搜狐博客的标识，搜狐博客更成为广大网民的网络之家。在短短的一年时间里，搜狐博客注册用户突破了1千万大关，经过千万网友的细心经营，搜狐博客再次迎来2007年度人物评选，经过激烈角逐，2007搜狐博客年度人物榜中榜评选活动终于尘埃落定，年度10大奖项被各大名博草根们收入囊中，他们是：搜狐年度博客刘翔、年度财经汪丁丁、年度娱乐博客李亚鹏、年度时尚博客仇明、年度IT博客周忆清、年度汽车超仁、年度医学博客顾建文、年度公益博客刘明胜、年度女人博客王秋杨、年度文化博客袁熙坤。当晚博客大会万人演唱会上，搜狐年度人物代表闪亮登场，与万民博友共度搜狐博客大会超级盛典。
万人演唱会群星璀璨
饕餮盛宴尽在搜狐博客
当晚，北京朝阳公园星光璀璨，搜狐第一博客达人――搜狐公司董事局主席兼首席执行官
张朝阳
先生拉开搜狐第二届博客大会暨搜狐3.0落成大典之万人演唱会的帷幕。林俊杰、羽泉、小柯、何洁、阿朵、黄圣依、叶蓓、瞿颖、胡灵、后舍男生、搜狗女声等络绎不绝的娱乐明星、网络达人、十大博客圈的名人名博们的华丽亮相，为万民搜狐博友献上了一场规模空前的群星演唱会。在场数百名嘉宾和万名博友的共同见证了这一历史性的时刻，福建东南卫视全程转播活动的盛况。
自2006年首届搜狐博客大会引爆博客“玩・弄”革命，并吸引无数明星、网络达人、名博现身搜狐博客大会与博友们狂欢后，搜狐博客便吸引了无数名人和草根在搜狐扎根。此次第二届搜狐博客大会可谓盛况空前，万众瞩目。瞿颖、叶蓓等参加过首届博客大会的明星名博再次前来鼎力助阵，更吸引了新加坡人气小天王林俊杰、羽泉、小柯、何洁等等诸多演艺界巨星加入狂欢盛典，超豪华的明星阵容同台献艺，放歌搜狐博客大会万人演唱会。令人目眩神迷的视觉桥段呈现出无尽的想像空间，劲曲热舞，倾情打造一场音乐的饕餮盛宴，搜狐博客大会成为万名搜狐博友的狂欢盛典。
长达8小时的搜狐博客大会酣畅淋漓的为万名博友呈现了一场超级盛宴，万民博友HIGH翻了京城之夜，在博友们流连忘返无尽回味中结束了搜狐独家为网民打造的超级盛典。搜狐“以人为本”的理念让用户切实感受到搜狐技术驱动带来的全新用户体验，这一切“不只是博客，得是搜狐博客”！
搜狐公司董事局主席兼首席执行官
张朝阳
先生表示，“经过三年多的开拓和积累，搜狐3.0已经全面落成。搜狐3.0的落成，标志着以技术和产品驱动的搜狐正在全面崛起。第二届搜狐博客大会将搜狐3.0从线上搬到线下，通过精心设置的交流互动环节让万名网友抢先体验搜狐3.0全线产品的强大功能，让网民切身感受到搜狐技术带来的全新的用户体验。在未来的时间里，随着搜狐3.0在网民的生活、工作、娱乐等方面的作用进一步加大，以及2008年奥运会的日益临近，搜狐正在迎接一个前所未有的高速而又稳健的发展阶段。在未来三到五年内，中国网民的数量将达到5亿，届时，搜狐将为大多数网民提供最主流的互联网服务，并成为中国最强大的两到三家互联网公司之一。”

Company
Profile
Sohu.com
Inc.
(NASDAQ: SOHU)
is
China's
premier
online
brand
and
indispensable
to
the
daily
life
of
millions
of
Chinese,
providing
a
network
of
web
properties
and
community
based/web
2.0
products
which
offer
the
vast
Sohu
user
community
a
broad
array
of
choices
regarding
information,
entertainment
and
communication.
Sohu
has
built
one
of
the
most
comprehensive
matrices
of
Chinese
language
web
properties
and
proprietary
search
engines,
consisting
of
seven
leading
web
properties.

2007
SOHU.COM
Reports
Second
Quarter
2007
Unaudited
Financial
Results
Second
Quarter
2007
Brand
Advertising
Revenues
Reach
US$26.6
million,
Exceeding
High
End
of
Guidance
by
US$1.6
Million,
Up
38%
Year-on-Year;
Second
Quarter
2007
Total
Revenues
Reach
US$39.0
million,
Exceeding
High
End
of
Guidance
by
US$1.5
Million,
Up
14%
Year-on-Year;
Second
Quarter
2007
Non-GAAP
Fully
Diluted
EPS
Is
US$0.21,
Exceeding
High
End
of
Guidance
BEIJING,
CHINA,
August
1,
2007
C
Sohu.com
Inc.
(NASDAQ: SOHU),
China's
leading
online
media,
search,
mobile
value-added
services
and
online
gaming
company,
today
reported
unaudited
financial
results
for
the
second
quarter
ended
June
30,
2007.
Second
Quarter
Highlights:
・
Record
brand
advertising
revenues
of
US$26.6
million,
up
38%
year-on-year
and
13%
quarter-on-quarter,
exceeding
company
guidance,
demonstrating
robust
momentum
in
advertisers’
spending
as
Sohu
enjoys
dominant
advantages
surrounding
the
Beijing
2008
Olympic
Games
・
Record
advertising
revenues
of
US$28.4
million,
up
24%
year-on-year
and
11%
quarter-on-quarter,
exceeding
company
guidance.
・
Non-advertising
revenue
of
US$10.6
million,
down
6%
year-on-year
and
up
42%
quarter-on-quarter,
exceeding
company
guidance.
・
Total
revenues
of
US$39.0
million,
up
14%
year-on-year
and
18%
quarter-on-quarter,
exceeding
company
guidance.
・
Non-GAAP
net
income
(i.e. excluding share-based compensation expenses)
of
US$8.1
million
or
US$0.21
per
fully
diluted
share,
exceeding
company
guidance.
・
GAAP
net
income
of
US$5.7
million
or
US$0.15
per
fully
diluted
share.
・
On
May
9,
the
Company
launched
its
in-house
developed
massive
multiplayer
online
role-playing
game
(MMORPG)
Tian
Long
Ba
Bu
(TLBB).
For
the
period
from
May
10
to
June
30,
2007,
TLBB
generated
revenues
of
US$2.3
million
with
peak
concurrent
users
exceeded
400,000.
・
On
July
21,
the
Company
debuted
Sohu
3.0,
a
comprehensive
package
of
fully
integrated
online
products
including
Sohu
Blog,
Sohu
Passport
and
Sohu
Web-based
Messenger.
・
Explanation
of
the
Company's
non-GAAP
financial
measures
and
the
related
reconciliations
to
GAAP
financial
measures
are
included
in
the
accompanying
“Non-GAAP
Disclosure”
and
the
“Reconciliation
to
Unaudited
Condensed
Consolidated
Statements
of
Operations.”
Dr.
Charles
Zhang,
Chairman
and
CEO
of
Sohu.com,
stated,
“We
are
pleased
to
report
outstanding
second
quarter
results
for
Sohu,
exceeding
our
expectations
in
each
of
our
revenue
categories
and
earnings.
Our
dominant
advantages
surrounding
the
Beijing
2008
Olympic
Games
C
as
official
Internet
Content
Sponsor
and
operator
of
beijing2008.cn,
exclusive
strategic
partner
of
China
Interactive
Sports,
and
exclusive
Internet
Content
Partner
for
Team
China
C
are
paying
off.
Advertising
revenue
momentum
continues
to
accelerate
as
our
unmatched
content
strength
brings
in
more
users,
increased
traffic
and
new
advertisers.”
Second
Quarter
Financial
Results
Total
revenues
for
second
quarter
ended
June
30,
2007
totaled
US$39.0
million,
compared
to
revenues
of
US$33.1
million
for
first
quarter
ended
March
31,
2007,
and
US$34.1
million
for
second
quarter
ended
June
30,
2006.
Gross
margin
of
61%
in
second
quarter
of
2007
increased
from
60%
in
the
previous
quarter
and
decreased
from
63%
in
the
same
period
of
2006.
Non-GAAP
gross
margin
was
62%
in
the
second
quarter
of
2007,
up
from
61%
in
the
previous
quarter
and
down
from
64%
in
the
same
period
of
2006.
Net
income
for
second
quarter
of
2007
was
US$5.7
million
or
US$0.15
per
fully
diluted
share.
Non-GAAP
net
income
for
second
quarter
of
2007
was
US$8.1
million
or
US$0.21
per
fully
diluted
share.
This
compares
to
non-GAAP
net
income
of
US$7.0
million
or
US$0.18
per
fully
diluted
share
for
first
quarter
2007
and
US$8.4
million
or
US$0.22
per
fully
diluted
share
for
second
quarter
of
2006
which
included
a
gain
on
early
redemption
of
convertible
notes
of
US$0.8
million.
Advertising
revenues
for
second
quarter
of
2007
totaled
US$28.4
million,
an
11%
quarter-on-quarter
increase
and
a
24%
year-on-year
increase.
Advertising
revenues,
consisting
of
US$26.6
million
in
brand
advertising
and
US$1.8
million
in
sponsored
search,
accounted
for
73%
of
total
revenues
in
the
second
quarter
of
2007.
Brand
advertising
revenues
for
second
quarter
of
2007
increased
13%
quarter-on-quarter
and
38%
year-on-year.
Sponsored
search
revenues
for
second
quarter
of
2007
decreased
16%
quarter-on-quarter
and
50%
year-on-year.
Advertising
gross
margin
for
second
quarter
of
2007
was
62%,
flat
with
the
previous
quarter
and
down
from
70%
in
the
second
quarter
of
2006.
Non-GAAP
advertising
gross
margin
for
second
quarter
of
2007
was
64%,
flat
with
the
previous
quarter
and
down
from
71%
in
the
second
quarter
of
2006.
For
the
second
quarter
of
2007,
Sohu's
non-advertising
revenues,
which
are
derived
mainly
from
wireless
value-added
services
and
online
games,
were
US$10.6
million,
representing
27%
of
total
revenues.
Non-advertising
gross
margin
was
56%,
compared
to
52%
in
the
previous
quarter
and
50%
in
second
quarter
of
2006.
Non-GAAP
non-advertising
gross
margin
was
56%,
compared
to
52%
in
the
previous
quarter
and
50%
in
second
quarter
of
2006.
The
increase
in
non-advertising
gross
margin
was
primarily
due
to
the
commercial
launch
of
TLBB.
For
second
quarter
of
2007,
Sohu's
operating
expenses
totaled
US$18.7
million.
Non-GAAP
operating
expenses
totaled
US$16.7
million,
an
increase
of
22%
from
the
previous
quarter
and
up
19%
year-on-year.
The
quarter-on-quarter
and
year-over-year
increases
were
mainly
due
to
continued
investment
in
product
development
and
Sohu
branding,
as
well
as
marketing
expenses
in
promoting
TLBB.
As
of
June
30,
2007,
Sohu's
balance
of
cash,
cash
equivalents
and
investments
in
marketable
debt
securities
was
US$113.1
million,
compared
to
US$97.5
million
and
US$129.7
million
as
of
March
31,
2007
and
December
31,
2006,
respectively.
Carol
Yu,
Co-President
and
CFO
of
Sohu.com,
commented,
“We
are
very
pleased
with
our
second
quarter
results.
We
look
forward
to
accelerating
momentum
during
the
run-up
to
the
Beijing
2008
Olympic
Games
through
continued
solid
execution
of
our
Olympic
strategy.
In
addition,
we
will
closely
monitor
progress
of
TLBB
and
strive
to
capitalize
on
its
initial
success.”
Business
Outlook
Sohu
estimates
total
revenues
for
third
quarter
2007
to
be
between
US$45
million
to
US$47
million,
with
advertising
revenues
of
US$30
million
to
US$31
million
and
non-advertising
revenues
of
US$15
million
to
US$16
million.
Sohu
estimates
brand
advertising
revenues
for
the
third
quarter
of
2007
to
be
between
US$28.5
million
to
US$29.5
million.
Sohu
estimates
non-GAAP
fully
diluted
earnings
per
share
for
the
third
quarter
of
2007
to
be
between
US$0.25
and
US$0.27.
Assuming
no
new
grants
of
share-based
awards,
Sohu
estimates
share-based
compensation
expense
for
the
third
quarter
of
2007
to
be
between
US$2.0
million
and
US$2.1
million.
The
estimated
impact
of
this
expense
is
expected
to
reduce
Sohu's
fully
diluted
earnings
per
share
for
the
third
quarter
of
2007,
under
US
GAAP,
by
US$0.05.
Non-GAAP
Disclosure
To
supplement
the
unaudited
consolidated
financial
statements
presented
in
accordance
with
United
States
Generally
Accepted
Accounting
Principles
(“GAAP”),
Sohu's
management
uses
non-GAAP
measures
of
cost
of
revenues,
operating
expenses,
net
income
and
net
income
per
share,
which
are
adjusted
from
results
based
on
GAAP
to
exclude
the
compensation
cost
of
share-based
awards
granted
to
employees
under
Statement
of
Financial
Accounting
Standard
123R,
effective
from
January
1,
2006.
These
measures
should
be
considered
in
addition
to
results
prepared
in
accordance
with
GAAP,
but
should
not
be
considered
a
substitute
for,
or
superior
to,
GAAP
results.
Sohu's
management
believes
excluding
the
share-based
compensation
expense
from
its
non-GAAP
financial
measure
is
useful
for
itself
and
investors.
Further,
the
amount
of
share-based
compensation
expense
cannot
be
anticipated
by
management
and
business
line
leaders
and
these
expenses
were
not
built
into
the
annual
budgets
and
quarterly
forecasts,
which
have
been
the
basis
for
information
Sohu
provides
to
analysts
and
investors
as
guidance
for
future
operating
performance.
As
share-based
compensation
expense
does
not
involve
any
upfront
or
subsequent
cash
outflow,
Sohu
does
not
factor
this
in
when
evaluating
and
approving
expenditures
or
when
determining
the
allocation
of
its
resources
to
its
business
segments.
As
a
result,
the
monthly
financial
results
for
internal
reporting
and
any
performance
measure
for
commission
and
bonus
are
based
on
non-GAAP
financial
measures
that
exclude
share-based
compensation
expense.
The
non-GAAP
financial
measures
are
provided
to
enhance
the
investors’
overall
understanding
of
Sohu's
current
financial
performance
and
prospects
for
the
future.
A
limitation
of
using
non-GAAP
cost
of
revenues,
operating
expenses,
net
income
and
net
income
per
share,
excluding
share-based
compensation
expenses
is
that
the
share-based
compensation
charge
has
been
and
will
continue
to
be
a
significant
recurring
expense
in
our
business
for
the
foreseeable
future.
In
order
to
mitigate
these
limitations
we
have
provided
specific
information
regarding
the
GAAP
amounts
excluded
from
each
non-GAAP
measure.
The
accompanying
tables
include
details
on
the
reconciliation
between
GAAP
financial
measures
that
are
most
directly
comparable
to
the
non-GAAP
financial
measures
we
have
presented.
Notes
to
Financial
Information
Financial
information
in
this
press
release
other
than
the
information
indicated
as
being
non-GAAP
is
extracted
from
Sohu's
unaudited
financial
statements
prepared
in
accordance
with
generally
accepted
accounting
principles
in
the
United
States.
On
June
20,
2006,
Sohu
discontinued
its
own
e-commerce
platform
of
physical
consumer
goods.
While
processing
the
disposal
of
its
e-commerce
business,
Sohu
is
reporting
the
related
business
activities
as
discontinued
operations.
Sohu's
income
statement
separates
out
discontinued
operations
for
both
current
and
prior
periods
in
order
to
focus
on
continuing
operations
and
provide
a
consistent
basis
for
comparing
financial
performance
over
time.
In
previous
quarters,
most
of
costs
and
expenses
for
the
game
department
were
related
to
product
development
and
research.
Accordingly,
Sohu
recorded
all
such
costs
and
expenses
in
product
development
expenses
in
its
statements
of
operations.
Beginning
April
1,
2007,
in
order
to
better
present
operation
results
to
enhance
comparability
with
industry
peers,
Sohu
reclassified
expenses
in
related
to
game
operations,
mainly
salary
and
benefits
of
game
masters,
from
product
development
expense
to
cost
of
online
game
revenues.
To
conform
with
current
period
presentations,
the
relevant
amounts
for
prior
periods
have
been
reclassified.
Such
reclassification
amounted
to
US$275,000
and
US$319,000
for
the
three
months
ended
March
31,
2007
and
June
30,
2006,
respectively,
and
amounted
to
US$642,000
for
the
six
months
ended
June
30,
2006.
Safe
Harbor
Statement
This
announcement
contains
forward-looking
statements.
It
is
currently
expected

搜狐动态
2007
搜狐公司公布2007年第二季度未经审计财务报告
2007年第二季度品牌广告收入达到2660万美元，比公司预期上限高出160万美元，
比上年同期增长38%;
2007年第二季度总收入达到3900万美元，比公司预期上限高出150万美元，
比上年同期增长14%;
2007年第二季度非美国通用会计准则每股摊薄净收益21美分，高于公司预期上限
中国北京，2007年8月1日
C
搜狐
(Nasdaq: SOHU)，中国领先的互联网媒体、搜索、移动增值服务及在线游戏公司，今天公布了未经审计的、截至2007年6月30日的2007年第二季度财务报告。
2007年第二季度重要业绩
-
品牌广告收入达到创记录的2660万美元，比去年同期增长38%，比上一季度增长13%，高于公司预期，显示出搜狐在北京2008年奥运会方面的绝对优势带来的强劲广告增长
-
广告收入达到创记录的2840万美元，比去年同期增长24%，比上一季度增长11%，高于公司预期
-
非广告收入1060万美元，比去年同期下降6%，比上一季度增长42%，高于公司预期
-
总收入3900万美元，比去年同期增长14%，比上一季度增长18%，高于公司预期
-
非美国通用会计准则净利润（即不包括股票激励的费用）为810万美元，即每股摊薄净收益21美分，高于公司预期
-
美国通用会计准则净利润570万美元，即每股摊薄净收益15美分
-
5月9日，推出自主研发的多角色扮演在线游戏“天龙八部”。从2007年5月10日至6月30日期间，天龙八部收入为230万美元，最高同时在线人数超过40万人
-
7月21日，推出搜狐3.0，将搜狐门户矩阵内各网站的内容和产品服务全部整合，包括搜狐博客、搜狐通行证和搜狐小纸条
-
关于公司非美国通用会计准则财务数据以及对应美国通用会计准则财务数据所做的相关调整的说明参见“非美国通用会计准则披露”的附注和“对未经审计的简要合并损益表调整表”
搜狐公司董事会主席兼首席执行官张朝阳先生说：“我们欣然宣布2007年第二季度业绩强劲，收入和利润均高于公司预期。搜狐在北京2008年奥运会方面具有绝对优势。我们是北京2008年奥运会互联网内容服务赞助商、北京2008年奥运会官方网站运营者、华奥星空独家战略合作伙伴以及中国体育代表团独家互联网内容合作伙伴。各种角色和身份使我们进一步壮大内容，带来更多用户、流量，以及新广告客户，从而使广告收入得以持续迅猛地增长。”
2007年第二季度财务业绩
截至2007年6月30日的2007年第二季度总收入为3900万美元，较之于截至2007年3月31日的2007年第一季度总收入为3310万美元，与截至2006年6月30日的2006年第二季度的总收入为3410万美元。
2007年第二季度的毛利率为61%，高于上季度的60%，低于2006年同期的63%。2007年第二季度的非美国通用会计准则毛利率为62%，高于上一季度的61%，低于2006年同期的64%。
2007年第二季度的净利润为570万美元，即每股摊薄净收益15美分。2007年第二季度的非美国通用会计准则净利润为810万美元，即每股摊薄净收益21美分，较之于2007年第一季度的非美国通用会计准则净利润700万美元，即每股摊薄净收益18美分，与2006年第二季度的非美国通用会计准则净利润840万美元（含提前赎回可转换债券收益80万美元），即每股摊薄净收益22美分。
2007年第二季度的广告收入为2840万美元，比上一季度增长11%，比去年同期增长24%。广告收入包括2660万美元的品牌广告收入和180万美元的付费搜索收入，共构成2007年第二季度总收入的73%。2007年第二季度的品牌广告收入比上季度增加13%，比去年同期增加38%。2007年度第二季度的付费搜索收入比上季度下降16%，比去年同期下降50%。2007年第二季度广告业务的毛利率为62%，与上季度持平，低于2006年第二季度的70%。2007年第二季度广告业务的非美国通用会计准则毛利率为64%，与上季度持平，低于2006年第二季度的71%。
2007年第二季度，搜狐公司的非广告收入为1060万美元，占总收入的27%，主要来自无线增值服务和在线游戏。非广告收入毛利率为56%，较之于上一季度的52％，与2006年第二季度的50%。非广告收入的非美国通用会计准则毛利率为56%，较之于上一季度的52％，与2006年第二季度的50%。非广告业务毛利率的上升主要是由于天龙八部的商业运营。
2007年第二季度，搜狐公司的营业费用为1870万美元。非美国通用会计准则营业费用为1670万美元，比上一季度增长22%，比去年同期增长19%。营业费用与上一季度和去年同期相比增长，主要是由于搜狐继续增加对研发和品牌推广的投入，以及对天龙八部的上线进行市场推广。
截止于2007年6月30日，搜狐公司的现金、现金等价物及可变现债券投资余额为1亿1310万美元，较之于2007年3月31日的9750万美元，和2006年12月31日的1亿2970万美元。
搜狐公司联席总裁兼首席财务官余楚媛女士说，“
我们对第二季度的业绩非常满意。随着北京2008年奥运会的临近，我们将通过持续有力地执行奥运战略，迎接搜狐公司的加速发展。此外，我们也会密切关注天龙八部的运营，致力于把已获得的初步成功转化为更佳收益。”
业务展望
搜狐公司预计2007年第三季度的总收入在4500万美元至4700万美元之间，其中广告收入为3000万美元至3100万美元之间，非广告收入为1500万美元至1600万美元之间。搜狐公司预计2007年第三季度的品牌广告收入在2850万美元至2950万美元之间。
搜狐公司预计2007年第三季度的非美国通用会计准则每股摊薄净收益为25美分至27美分之间。
假设在不增发其他股票激励的情况下，搜狐预计2007年第三季度的股票激励的费用在200万美元至210万美元之间。该项费用预期将使搜狐公司2007年第三季度的美国通用会计准则每股摊薄净收益减少5美分。
非美国通用会计准则披露
作为对遵照美国通用会计准则提交的未经审计的合并财务报表的补充，搜狐公司管理层提供了非美国通用会计准则成本、经营费用、净利润和每股净收益，即将2006年1月1日起生效的SFAS123R规定股票激励的费用从美国通用会计准则数据中调整出。提供非美国通用会计准则财务数据旨在加强投资者对搜狐公司当前财务业绩和未来前景的总体理解。这些数据应被视为对遵照美国通用会计准则编制的财务报告的补充，而不应被视为可代替或优于美国通用会计准则数据。
搜狐公司管理层认为，不包括股票激励费用的非美国通用会计准则净收入对其本身和投资者都有其用处。并且，公司管理层和业务领导无法预计股票激励费用的金额，公司做年度预算和季度预测，即提供给投资者和分析师的业务展望的基础时也不考虑这部分费用。由于股票激励费用不涉及任何过去或将来的现金流，搜狐在评估和审批费用支出以及分配资源至各业务部门时都不会考虑此因素。因此，各月的内部财务报告和所有的绩效奖励考核都是基于不含股票激励费用的非美国通用会计准则进行的。
非美国通用会计准则财务数据帮助投资者了解搜狐目前的财务状况和对未来的展望。使用非美国通用会计准则的成本、经营费用、净利润和每股净收益也有其不足之处，股票激励费用已经是而且在可预见的将来也会是我们业务中一项重大持续费用。为了弥补这部分不足，我们同时提供了关于美国通用会计准则金额和非美国通用会计准则差别的具体信息。在后文的附表里列示了美国通用会计准则和非美国通用会计准则调整的明细，可以直观地进行比较。
财务报告附注
本财务报告中的财务信息（不包括非美国通用会计准则财务信息）是从按照美国通用会计准则准备的未经审计的搜狐公司财务报表中摘录的。
2006年6月20日起，搜狐公司终止运营其电子商务平台，并将相关业务视为终止经营业务。为了使读者更关注持续经营业务，并保持财务数据的一致性，搜狐公司本期和以前期间的损益表中将单独披露终止经营业务。
在以前报告期间内，游戏部门的大部分成本和费用都是为产品开发而发生。相应地，公司将所有发生的费用记录在产品开发费用当中。自2007年4月1日开始，为了更好地反映运营绩效以进一步加强与同业的可比性，搜狐对与游戏运营相关的费用进行了重分类调整，主要是将游戏运营人员的薪酬福利费用从产品开发费用重分类至在线游戏业务的成本中。相应地，为保持与当前报告期间一致，公司也对以前报告期间公布的相关数据进行了重分类调整。上述重分类在2007年第一季度和2006年第二季度的金额分别为27.5万美元和31.9万美元，在2006年上半年的金额为64.2万美元。
有关前瞻性陈述的警告声明
本财务报告中包含前瞻性的陈述。我们现在预期“业务展望”中的内容在下个季度财务报告公布之前不会被更新。但是，搜狐公司保留在任何时候，由于任何原因对“业务展望”部分的内容进行更新的权利。
非历史事实的陈述，包括关于我们的信念及预期的陈述，均为前瞻性陈述。这些陈述是基于当前的计划，估计及预期，请不要对其产生不适当的依赖。前瞻性的陈述中包含风险及不确定因素。我们提醒您一些重要的因素会导致实际结果与前瞻性陈述有重大差别。潜在的风险及不确定因素包括但不限于：中华人民共和国产业政策的不确定、各季度运营结果可能出现上下波动、搜狐公司过去及未来可能的亏损、有限的营业历史、以及本公司仰赖在线广告销售、无线业务（其收入主要通过数家移动电信运营商取得）和在线游戏作为主要收入来源的事实。更多有关上述及其他风险的资讯收录于截至2006年12月31日的搜狐公司年报和10-K表格，以及向美国证券交易委员会提交的其他文件中。
电话会议
搜狐公司将于2007年8月1日周三股市收盘后公布截至2007年6月30日的2007年第二季度未经审计的财务报告。之后，公司管理层将于美国东部时间2007年8月1日晚8点（即北京/ 香港时间2007年8月2日上午8点）举行电话会议，讨论2007年第二季度的财务业绩。

关于搜狐公司
搜狐公司
(NASDAQ: SOHU)是中国领先的互联网品牌，是中国人生活中不可缺少的一部分，搜狐的网络资产以及基于web2.0产品的社区给众多的SOHU用户在信息、娱乐、交流、商务领域提供了非常广泛的选择可能。SOHU建立了中国最全面的互联网资产组合之一和自有搜索引擎，其中包括最大的门户和中国领先的互联网媒体网站
www.sohu.com；互动搜索引擎www.sogou.com；中国第一在线校友录www.chinaren.com；中国第一网络游戏信息门户
www.17173.com；顶尖的房地产网站www.focus.cn；无线移动增值服务提供商
www.goodfeel.com.cn；以及领先的地图服务提供商www.go2map.com。
搜狐公司的企业客户服务包括在其网络矩阵上投放的在线广告以及在其自主研发的搜索引擎上投放的付费搜索和竞价搜索广告服务。搜狐公司还提供个人用户服务：包括基于手机的新闻、资讯、音乐、铃声和图片下载等无线增值服务，两款多角色扮演在线游戏《天龙八部》和《刀剑》，以及一个休闲游戏平台。搜狐公司由中国互联网先驱张朝阳(张朝阳博客,张朝阳新闻,张朝阳说吧)先生创办，已经成功运作十一年。

搜狐公司
搜狐动态
2007
搜狐公司晋升方刚先生为产品副总裁
（2007年8月8日，北京）中国最领先的新媒体、通信及互动娱乐公司搜狐公司（NASDAQ:SOHU）宣布，经董事会及公司管理层决定并批准，自2007年7月1日起，搜狐公司产品技术中心高级总监方刚晋升为搜狐公司产品副总裁，进入公司高层管理团队。
方刚先生在搜狐博客的创立和发展过程中功勋卓著，且在互动产品方面做出了杰出贡献。搜狐自2005年9月正式推出博客服务，搜狐博客的产品、技术和运营团队在方刚先生的带领下，经过先后经历了2006“玩&#8226;弄”版、2007“声&#8226;色”版，成功地改写了中文博客的定义。目前，搜狐博客已经成为国内功能最全、个性化最强、最受欢迎的个人博客空间。
搜狐公司董事局主席兼首席执行官张朝阳先生欣慰地表示，“祝贺方刚晋升为产品副总裁，这也是搜狐首次设立产品副总裁职务。技术驱动和产品导向战略是搜狐未来发展的重要引擎之一，方刚先生的晋升，体现了搜狐对产品、技术、用户体验孜孜追求的理念。”
方刚先生对搜狐的产品发展充满了信心，他表示，“搜狐拥有国内最领先的互联网技术和产品团队，我相信，搜狐的网络产品和服务将成为中文互联网用户的主流选择。”
附：方刚先生简历
方刚
搜狐公司副总裁
方刚先生负责搜狐公司的互动产品
方刚先生毕业于清华大学，先后获工学学士学位和文学学士学位。
1999年6月，参与筹办赛迪网，曾任赛迪网总编、副总裁。
2003年8月，加入搜狐公司，任搜狐网副总编，产经中心总监。
2006年4月1日，任搜狐公司产品技术高级总监。
2007年7月1日，晋升为搜狐公司产品副总裁，进入公司高层管理团队。

About
Sohu.com
Sohu.com
Inc.
(NASDAQ: SOHU)
is
China's
premier
online
brand
and
indispensable
to
the
daily
life
of
millions
of
Chinese,
providing
a
network
of
web
properties
and
community
based/web
2.0
products
which
offer
the
vast
Sohu
user
community
a
broad
array
of
choices
regarding
information,
entertainment
and
communication.
Sohu
has
built
one
of
the
most
comprehensive
matrices
of
Chinese
language
web
properties
and
proprietary
search
engines,
consisting
of
the
mass
portal
and
leading
online
media
destination
www.sohu.com;
interactive
search
engine
www.sogou.com;
#1
online
alumni
club
www.chinaren.com;
#1
games
information
portal
www.17173.com;
the
top
real
estate
website
www.focus.cn;
wireless
value-added
services
provider
www.goodfeel.com.cn;
and
leading
online
mapping
service
provider
www.go2map.com.
Sohu
corporate
services
consist
of
brand
advertising
on
its
matrix
of
websites
as
well
as
paid
listing
and
bid
listing
on
its
in-house
developed
search
directory
and
engines.
Sohu
also
offers
two
types
of
consumer
services.
Sohu
offers
wireless
value-added
services
such
as
news,
information,
music,
ringtone
and
picture
content
sent
over
mobile
phones.
The
company
also
operates
two
massive
multi-player
online
role-playing
games
and
a
casual
game
platform.
Sohu.com,
established
by
Dr.
Charles
Zhang,
one
of
China's
Internet
pioneers,
is
in
its
eleventh
year
of
operation.

Information

SOHU.COM
Reports
Third
Quarter
2007
Unaudited
Financial
Results
Third
Quarter
2007
Brand
Advertising
Revenues
Reach
US$29.8
million,
Exceeding
Guidance
and
Up
42%
Year-on-Year;
Third
Quarter
2007
Online
Games
Revenues
Reach
US$12.7
million,
Up
473%
Year-on-Year;
Third
Quarter
2007
Total
Revenues
Reach
US$51.5
million,
Exceeding
High
End
of
Guidance
by
US$4.5
million,
Up
46%
Year-on-Year;
Third
Quarter
2007
Non-GAAP
Fully
Diluted
EPS
of
US$0.30,
Exceeding
High
End
of
Guidance
by
3
US
Cents
BEIJING,
CHINA,
October
29,
2007
C
Sohu.com
Inc.
(NASDAQ: SOHU),
China's
leading
online
media,
communications,
search,
online
gaming
and
mobile
value-added
services
company,
today
reported
unaudited
financial
results
for
the
third
quarter
ended
September
30,
2007.
Third
Quarter
Highlights
&#8226;Record
high
total
revenues
and
record
high
for
each
revenue
category:
brand
advertising,
advertising,
and
non-advertising
revenues
as
well
as
non-GAAP
net
income.
All
such
operating
parameters
exceed
company
guidance.
&#8226;Brand
advertising
revenues
of
US$29.8
million,
up
42%
year-on-year
and
12%
quarter-on-quarter.
&#8226;Advertising
revenues
of
US$31.5
million,
up
32%
year-on-year
and
11%
quarter-on-quarter.
&#8226;Online
games
revenues
of
US$12.7
million,
up
473%
year-on-year
and
232%
quarter-on-quarter.
In-house
developed
massive
multiplayer
online
role-playing
game
Tian
Long
Ba
Bu
(TLBB)
solidified
its
success
with
revenue
up
384%
quarter-on-quarter
to
US$10.9
million.
&#8226;Non-advertising
revenues
of
US$20.0
million,
up
74%
year-on-year
and
88%
quarter-on-quarter.
&#8226;Total
revenues
of
US$51.5
million,
up
46%
year-on-year
and
32%
quarter-on-quarter,
exceeding
company
guidance
by
US$4.5
million.
&#8226;Non-GAAP
net
income
(i.e. excluding share-based compensation expenses)
of
US$11.7
million
or
US$0.30
per
fully
diluted
share,
exceeding
company
guidance
by
3
US
cents.
Non-GAAP
net
income
increased
37%
year-on-year
and
44%
quarter-on-quarter.
&#8226;GAAP
net
income
of
US$9.7
million
or
US$0.25
per
fully
diluted
share.
GAAP
net
income
increased
47%
year-on-year
and
70%
quarter-on-quarter.
&#8226;Explanation
of
the
Company's
non-GAAP
financial
measures
and
the
related
reconciliations
to
GAAP
financial
measures
are
included
in
the
accompanying
“Non-GAAP
Disclosure”
and
the
“Reconciliations
to
Unaudited
Condensed
Consolidated
Statements
of
Operations.”
Dr.
Charles
Zhang,
Chairman
and
CEO
of
Sohu.com,
stated,
“I
am
very
pleased
to
report
another
outstanding
quarter
with
record
total
revenues
and
non-GAAP
earnings.
We
have
exceeded
all
of
our
guidance
for
each
of
our
revenue
categories
as
well
as
earnings.
This
set
of
results
are
made
possible
only
because
of
our
focus
on
technology
and
our
long-term
vision,
such
as
our
investment
in
our
first
in-house
developed
online
game
Tian
Long
Ba
Bu
and
our
Beijing
2008
Olympics
sponsorship.
Our
other
technological
initiatives,
including
Sohu
3.0
launched
during
late
July,
Sogou
Pinyin,
are
all
progressing
well.
Our
unmatched
reporting
on
the
“One
Year
Countdown
to
Beijing
2008
Olympics”
and
successful
rehearsal
to
“Olympic
Torch
Relay
Cross
Mount
Everest”
through
on-site
reporting
at
the
6178
meters
high
Yuzhu
Mountain
during
the
National
Day
Holiday,
have
further
solidified
our
undisputed
position
as
the
“Portal
of
Choice
for
the
Beijing
Olympics”.”
Ms.
Belinda
Wang,
Co-President
and
Chief
Marketing
Office
of
Sohu.com,
said,
“Fueled
by
the
fast
growth
of
China
economy
and
continued
migration
of
advertisers
from
offline
to
online,
our
brand
advertising
business
continues
to
ride
the
tide
of
a
robust
market,
especially
with
the
Beijing
2008
Olympic
Games
now
less
than
ten
months
away.
In
the
third
quarter,
we
delivered
record
high
brand
advertising
revenue
of
$29.8
million,
representing
42%
year-on-year
growth.
For
the
first
nine
months
of
2007,
brand
advertising
revenue
grew
by
40%
year-on-year,
despite
a
challenging
comparison
to
2006
with
the
FIFA
World
Cup.”
Dr.
Gong
Yu,
Chief
Operating
Officer
of
Sohu.com,
added,
“On
the
content
side,
with
increased
broadband
penetration
and
continuous
improvement
of
peer-to-peer
streaming
technology,
online
video
content
is
now
in
even
higher
demand
from
Internet
users.
To
expand
our
video
services,
we
have
launched
a
new
“TV
channel”
through
strategic
partnerships
with
49
television
stations.
Programs
from
these
TV
stations
are
now
streamed
on
Sohu.
Such
TV
clips
are
nicely
integrated
into
our
text-based
content
and
have
been
well
received
by
our
users.”
Third
Quarter
Financial
Results
Total
revenues
for
third
quarter
ended
September
30,
2007
were
US$51.5
million,
compared
to
revenues
of
US$39.0
million
for
second
quarter
ended
June
30,
2007,
and
US$35.4
million
for
third
quarter
ended
September
30,
2006.
Gross
margin
of
67%
in
third
quarter
of
2007
increased
from
61%
in
the
previous
quarter
and
64%
in
the
same
period
of
2006.
Non-GAAP
gross
margin
was
67%
in
the
third
quarter
of
2007,
up
from
62%
in
the
previous
quarter
and
65%
in
the
same
period
of
2006.
The
gross
margin
expansion
was
primarily
due
to
the
contribution
from
TLBB.
Net
income
for
third
quarter
of
2007
was
US$9.7
million
or
US$0.25
per
fully
diluted
share.
Non-GAAP
net
income
for
third
quarter
of
2007
was
US$11.7
million
or
US$0.30
per
fully
diluted
share.
This
compares
to
non-GAAP
net
income
of
US$8.1
million
or
US$0.21
per
fully
diluted
share
for
second
quarter
of
2007
and
US$8.5
million
or
US$0.22
per
fully
diluted
share
for
third
quarter
of
2006.
Advertising
revenues
for
third
quarter
of
2007
totaled
US$31.5
million,
an
11%
quarter-on-quarter
increase
and
a
32%
year-on-year
increase.
Advertising
revenues,
consisting
of
US$29.8
million
in
brand
advertising
and
US$1.7
million
in
sponsored
search,
accounted
for
61%
of
total
revenues
in
the
third
quarter
of
2007.
Brand
advertising
revenues
for
third
quarter
of
2007
increased
12%
quarter-on-quarter
and
42%
year-on-year.
Sponsored
search
revenues
for
third
quarter
of
2007
were
flat
quarter-on-quarter
and
decreased
39%
year-on-year.
Advertising
gross
margin
for
third
quarter
of
2007
was
63%,
up
from
62%
for
the
previous
quarter
and
down
from
69%
in
the
third
quarter
of
2006.
Non-GAAP
advertising
gross
margin
for
third
quarter
of
2007
was
64%,
flat
with
the
previous
quarter
and
down
from
71%
in
the
third
quarter
of
2006.
The
year-on-year
decrease
was
mainly
due
to
increased
content
costs,
bandwidth
and
server
depreciation
expenses.
For
the
third
quarter
of
2007,
Sohu's
non-advertising
revenues,
which
are
derived
mainly
from
online
games
and
wireless
value-added
services,
were
US$20.0
million,
representing
39%
of
total
revenues.
Online
games
revenues
for
third
quarter
of
2007
increased
232%
quarter-on-quarter
and
473%
year-on-year.
Wireless
revenue
increased
4%
quarter-on-quarter
and
decreased
23%
year-on-year.
Non-advertising
gross
margin
was
72%,
compared
to
56%
in
the
previous
quarter
and
54%
in
third
quarter
of
2006.
Non-GAAP
non-advertising
gross
margin
was
72%,
compared
to
56%
in
the
previous
quarter
and
54%
in
third
quarter
of
2006.
Those
increases
were
due
to
the
contribution
from
TLBB.
For
third
quarter
of
2007,
Sohu's
operating
expenses
totaled
US$25.6
million.
Non-GAAP
operating
expenses
totaled
US$23.9
million,
an
increase
of
43%
from
the
previous
quarter
and
up
58%
year-on-year.
The
increase
was
primarily
due
to
continued
investment
in
product
development
and
Sohu
branding,
marketing
expenses
for
TLBB
and
Sohu
3.0,
as
well
as
an
increase
in
bonuses
to
reward
employees
for
their
contribution
to
good
results.
In
third
quarter
2007,
Sohu
disposed
its
equity
interest
in
an
associated
company,
resulted
in
a
gain
of
$0.6
million.
As
of
September
30,
2007,
subsequent
to
the
redemption
of
its
zero
coupon
convertible
senior
notes
of
$58.5
million
in
July
2007,
Sohu's
balance
of
cash,
cash
equivalents
and
investments
in
marketable
debt
securities
remained
at
a
comfortable
level
of
US$76.9
million,
compared
to
US$113.1
million
and
US$129.7
million
as
of
June
30,
2007
and
December
31,
2006,
respectively.
Ms.
Carol
Yu,
Co-President
and
CFO
of
Sohu.com,
commented,
“Management’s
focus
on
technology
and
long-term
vision
over
the
last
few
years
have
started
to
pay
off.
Investments
in
our
in-house
developed
game,
Tian
Long
Ba
Bu,
our
Olympic
sponsorship
and
our
stock
repurchase
programs
(under which we repurchased 2.9 million shares since 2004, at an average price of US$18.2)
have
now
been
proven
to
be
decisions
that
contribute
to
the
long-term
benefit
of
the
company
and
to
the
enhancement
of
shareholder
value.”
Business
Outlook
Sohu
estimates
total
revenues
for
the
fourth
quarter
2007
to
be
between
US$53.5million
to
US$55.5
million,
with
advertising
revenues
of
US$31
million
to
US$32
million
and
non-advertising
revenues
of
US$22.5
million
to
US$23.5
million.
Sohu
estimates
brand
advertising
revenues
for
the
fourth
quarter
of
2007
to
be
between
US$29.5
million
to
US$30.5
million.
Sohu
estimates
non-GAAP
fully
diluted
earnings
per
share
for
the
fourth
quarter
of
2007
to
be
between
US$0.33
and
US$0.35.
Assuming
no
new
grants
of
share-based
awards,
Sohu
estimates
share-based
compensation
expense
for
the
fourth
quarter
of
2007
to
be
between
US$1.8
million
and
US$1.9
million.
The
estimated
impact
of
this
expense
is
expected
to
reduce
Sohu's
fully
diluted
earnings
per
share
for
the
fourth
quarter
of
2007,
under
US
GAAP,
by
US$0.05.
Non-GAAP
Disclosure
To
supplement
the
unaudited
consolidated
financial
statements
presented
in
accordance
with
United
States
Generally
Accepted
Accounting
Principles
(“GAAP”),
Sohu's
management
uses
non-GAAP
measures
of
cost
of
revenues,
operating
expenses,
net
income
and
net
income
per
share,
which
are
adjusted
from
results
based
on
GAAP
to
exclude
the
compensation
cost
of
share-based
awards
granted
to
employees
under
Statement
of
Financial
Accounting
Standard
123R,
effective
from
January
1,
2006.
These
measures
should
be
considered
in
addition
to
results
prepared
in
accordance
with
GAAP,
but
should
not
be
considered
a
substitute
for,
or
superior
to,
GAAP
results.
Sohu's
management
believes
excluding
the
share-based
compensation
expense
from
its
non-GAAP
financial
measure
is
useful
for
itself
and
investors.
Further,
the
amount
of
share-based
compensation
expense
cannot
be
anticipated
by
management
and
business
line
leaders
and
these
expenses
were
not
built
into
the
annual
budgets
and
quarterly
forecasts,
which
have
been
the
basis
for
information
Sohu
provides
to
analysts
and
investors
as
guidance
for
future
operating
performance.
As
share-based
compensation
expense
does
not
involve
any
upfront
or
subsequent
cash
outflow,
Sohu
does
not
factor
this
in
when
evaluating
and
approving
expenditures
or
when
determining
the
allocation
of
its
resources
to
its
business
segments.
As
a
result,
the
monthly
financial
results
for
internal
reporting
and
any
performance
measure
for
commission
and
bonus
are
based
on
non-GAAP
financial
measures
that
exclude
share-based
compensation
expense.
The
non-GAAP
financial
measures
are
provided
to
enhance
the
investors’
overall
understanding
of
Sohu's
current
financial
performance
and
prospects
for
the
future.
A
limitation
of
using
non-GAAP
cost
of
revenues,
operating
expenses,
net
income
and
net
income
per
share,
excluding
share-based
compensation
expenses
is
that
the
share-based
compensation
charge
has
been
and
will
continue
to
be
a
significant
recurring
expense
in
our
business
for
the
foreseeable
future.
In
order
to
mitigate
these
limitations
we
have
provided
specific
information
regarding
the
GAAP
amounts
excluded
from
each
non-GAAP
measure.
The
accompanying
tables
include
details
on
the
reconciliation
between
GAAP
financial
measures
that
are
most
directly
comparable
to
the
non-GAAP
financial
measures
we
have
presented.
Notes
to
Financial
Information
Financial
information
in
this
press
release
other
than
the
information
indicated
as
being
non-GAAP
is
extracted
from
Sohu's
unaudited
financial
statements
prepared
in
accordance
with
generally
accepted
accounting
principles
in
the
United
States.
On
June
20,
2006,
Sohu
discontinued
its
own
e-commerce
platform
of
physical
consumer
goods.
While
processing
the
disposal
of
its
e-commerce
business,
Sohu
is
reporting
the
related
business
activities
as
discontinued
operations.
Sohu's
income
statement
separates
out
discontinued
operations
for
both
current
and
prior
periods
in
order
to
focus
on
continuing
operations
and
provide
a
consistent
basis
for
comparing
financial
performance
over
time.
In
those
quarters
prior
to
April
1,
2007,
most
of
costs
and
expenses
for
the
game
department
were
related
to
product
development
and
research.
Accordingly,
Sohu
recorded
all
such
costs
and
expenses
in
product
development
expenses
in
its
statements
of
operations.
Beginning
April
1,
2007,
in
order
to
better
present
operation
results
to
enhance
comparability
with
industry
peers,
Sohu
reclassified
expenses
in
related
to
game
operations,
mainly
salary
and
benefits
of
game
masters,
from
product
development
expense
to
cost
of
online
game
revenues.
To
conform
with
current
period
presentations,
the
relevant
amounts
for
prior
periods
have
been
reclassified.
Such
reclassification
amounted
to
US$296,000
for
the
three
months
ended
September
30,
2006,
and
amounted
to
US$938,000
for
the
nine
months
ended
September
30,
2006.

Harbor
Statement

announcement

statements.

Outlook

Outlook

for
any
reason.
Statements
that
are
not

including

about

beliefs
and
expectations,
are
forward-looking
statements.
These
statements
are
based
on
current
plans,
estimates
and
projections,
and
therefore
you
should
not
place
undue
reliance
on

Forward-looking
statements
involve
inherent
risks
and
uncertainties.
We
caution
you
that
a
number

important
factors
could
cause

results
to

in

of
China,

in

and

(most wireless revenues are collected from a few mobile network operators)

搜狐公司
搜狐动态
2007
搜狐公司公布2007年第三季度未经审计财务报告
2007年第三季度品牌广告收入达到2980万美元，高于公司预期，
比上年同期增长42%;
2007年第三季度在线游戏收入达到1270万美元，
比上年同期增长
473%;
2007年第三季度总收入达到5150万美元，比公司预期上限高出450万美元，
比上年同期增长
46%;
2007年第三季度非美国通用会计准则每股摊薄净收益30美分
，比公司预期上限高出3美分
中国北京，
2007年10月29日
C
搜狐
(Nasdaq: SOHU)，中国领先的互联网媒体、搜索、在线游戏及移动增值服务公司，今天公布了截至
2007年9月30日
的未经审计的2007年第三季度财务报告。
2007
年第三季度重要业绩
-
创纪录的总收入和各个类别的收入，包括品牌广告、广告和非广告收入，以及创纪录的非美国通用会计准则净利润。同时，这些指标均高于公司预期。
-
品牌广告收入达到2980万美元，比去年同期增长42%，比上一季度增长12%。
-
广告收入达到3150万美元，比去年同期增长32%，比上一季度增长11%。
-
在线游戏收入达到1270万美元，比去年同期增长473%，比上一季度增长232%。自主研发的在线游戏“天龙八部”收入达到1090万美元，比上一季度增长384%
，进一步巩固了它的成功。
-
非广告收入达到2000万美元，比去年同期增长74%，比上一季度增长88%。
-
总收入达到5150万美元，比去年同期增长46%，比上一季度增长32%，比公司预期上限高出450万美元。
-
非美国通用会计准则净利润（即不包括股票激励的费用）达到1170万美元，即每股摊薄净收益30美分，高于公司预期3美分，比去年同期增长37%，比上一季度增长44%。
-
美国通用会计准则净利润970万美元，即每股摊薄净收益25美分，比去年同期增长47%，比上一季度增长70%。
-
关于对公司非美国通用会计准则财务数据的说明，以及其与美国通用会计准则财务数据之间的相关调节事项参见“非美国通用会计准则披露”的附注和“未经审计的简要合并损益表调节表”。
搜狐公司董事会主席兼首席执行官
张朝阳
先生说：“我很高兴地宣布这又是一个很出色的季度，总收入和非美国通用会计准则利润均创纪录。我们业务的收入和利润均超过了我们的所有预期。这直接得益于搜狐一贯致力技术研发与创新，以及我们的远见卓识，例如我们自主研发了第一款多角色扮演在线游戏“天龙八部”，以及我们赞助北京2008年奥运会并成为独家互联网内容服务赞助商。我们的技术创造，比如七月底上线的搜狐
3.0和搜狗拼音输入法都有良好的进展。我们对于奥运倒计时一周年活动进行的无可匹敌的报道以及为明年报道火炬上珠峰而在十一期间成功登顶海拔
6200米
的玉珠峰并进行报道演练，都更加表明我们将毫无争议地成为“首选的奥运会门户网站”。”
搜狐公司联席总裁兼首席营销官
王昕
女士说：“得益于中国经济的快速增长和广告形式更多的由线下广告转为线上广告，尤其是目前距离北京2008年奥运会只有不到十个月的时间，品牌广告业务正随着市场蓬勃增长。第三季度，我们的品牌广告收入达到创纪录的2980万美元，比去年同期增长42%。尽管在2006年有世界杯收入使得比较基数较高，与去年同期相比，在2007年的前九个月里品牌广告收入仍增长了40%。”
搜狐公司首席运营官
龚宇
博士说：“在内容方面，随着宽带普及率的提高和P2P流媒体技术的不断进步，互联网用户对网络视频内容有了更高的要求。为了扩展我们的视频服务，我们与49家电视台合作推出了一个新频道“看视频频道”，使他们的节目在搜狐的网络平台上播出。这类电视节目与我们的文字内容很好地结合在一起并深受用户的欢迎。”
2007
年第三季度
财务业绩
2007年第三季度（截至
2007年9月30日
）总收入为5150万美元，而2007年第二季度（截至
2007年6月30日
）的总收入为3900万美元，
2006年第三季度（截至
2006年9月30日
）的总收入为3540万美元。
2007年第三季度的毛利率为67%，高于上季度的61%
以及2006年同期的64%。2007年第三季度的非美国通用会计准则毛利率为67%，高于上一季度的62%
以及2006年同期的65%。毛利率的上升主要得益于“天龙八部”收入的增长。
2007年第三季度的净利润为970万美元，即每股摊薄净收益25美分。2007年第三季度的非美国通用会计准则净利润为1170万美元，即每股摊薄净收益30美分。而2007年第二季度的非美国通用会计准则净利润为810万美元，即每股摊薄净收益21美分，2006年第三季度的非美国通用会计准则净利润为850万美元，即每股摊薄净收益22美分。
2007年第三季度的广告收入为3150万美元，比上一季度增长11%，比去年同期增长32%。广告收入，包括2980万美元的品牌广告收入和170万美元的付费搜索收入，占2007年第三季度总收入的61%。2007年第三季度的品牌广告收入比上季度增长12%，比去年同期增长42%。2007年度第三季度的付费搜索收入与上季度持平，比去年同期下降39%。2007年第三季度广告业务的毛利率为63%，高于上季度的62%，低于2006年第三季度的69%。2007年第三季度广告业务的非美国通用会计准则毛利率为64%，与上季度持平，低于2006年第三季度的71%。毛利率与去年相比下降主要是由于内容成本、带宽成本和服务器折旧成本的上升。
2007年第三季度，搜狐公司的非广告收入为2000万美元，占总收入的39%，主要来自在线游戏和无线增值服务。2007年第三季度的在线游戏收入比上一季度增长232%，比去年同期增长473%。2007年第三季度的无线业务收入比上一季度增长4%，比去年同期下降23%。非广告收入毛利率为72%，而上一季度为56%，2006年第三季度为54%。非广告收入的非美国通用会计准则毛利率为72%，而上一季度为56%，2006年第三季度为54%，增长主要是受益于“天龙八部”的贡献。
2007年第三季度，搜狐公司的营业费用为2560万美元。非美国通用会计准则营业费用为2390万美元，比上一季度增长43%，比去年同期增长58%。营业费用的增长主要是由于搜狐对产品研发和搜狐品牌的持续投入，对“天龙八部”及搜狐3.0的市场推广费用，以及由于业绩出色增加了对员工的奖励。
2007年第三季度，我们出售了一项对参股公司的投资，收益60万美元。
我们于2007年7月赎回了5850万美元的可转债。截至
2007年9月30日
，搜狐公司的现金、现金等价物及可变现债券投资的余额为7690万美元，处于健康水平。
2007年6月30日
的现金、现金等价物及可变现债券投资的余额为1.131亿美元，
2006年12月31日
为1.297亿美元。
搜狐公司联席总裁兼首席财务官
余楚媛
女士说，“近几年管理层不断致力于技术创新和长期的发展战略开始带来回报。事实证明，我们对自主研发的“天龙八部”和对奥运会赞助商身份的投资，以及我们的股权回购计划（我们在此计划下，自2004年以来以平均18.2美元的价格回购了约290万股的公司股票）都为公司带来了长远的利益，并进一步为股东创造了价值。”
业务展望
搜狐公司预计2007年第四季度的总收入在5350万美元至5550万美元之间，其中广告收入为3100万美元至3200万美元之间，非广告收入为2250万美元至2350万美元之间。搜狐公司预计2007年第四季度的品牌广告收入在2950万美元至3050万美元之间。
搜狐公司预计2007年第四季度的非美国通用会计准则每股摊薄净收益在33美分至35美分之间。
假设在不增发其他股票激励的情况下，搜狐公司预计2007年第四季度的股票激励的费用在180万美元至190万美元之间。预期该项费用将使搜狐公司2007年第四季度的美国通用会计准则每股摊薄净收益减少5美分。
非美国通用会计准则披露
作为对遵照美国通用会计准则提交的未经审计的合并财务报表的补充，搜狐公司管理层提供了非美国通用会计准则成本、经营费用、净利润和每股净收益，即将
2006年1月1日起
生效的SFAS123R规定的股票激励的费用从美国通用会计准则数据中调整出来。提供非美国通用会计准则财务数据旨在加强投资者对搜狐公司当前财务业绩和未来前景的总体理解。这些数据应被视为对遵照美国通用会计准则编制的财务报告的补充，而不应被视为可代替或优于美国通用会计准则数据。
搜狐公司管理层认为，不包括股票激励费用的非美国通用会计准则净收入对其本身和投资者都有用处。并且，公司管理层和业务线领导无法预计股票激励费用的金额，因此作为搜狐公司提供给投资者和分析师的业务展望数据，公司年度预算和季度预测，在编制时也不考虑这部分费用。由于股票激励费用不涉及任何过去或将来的现金流，搜狐公司在评估和审批费用支出以及分配资源至各业务部门时都不会考虑此因素。因此，各月的内部财务报告和所有的绩效奖励考核都是基于不含股票激励费用的非美国通用会计准则进行的。
非美国通用会计准则财务数据帮助投资者了解搜狐目前的财务状况和对未来的展望。使用非美国通用会计准则的成本、经营费用、净利润和每股净收益也有其不足之处，股票激励费用已经是而且在可预见的将来也会是我们业务中一项重大持续费用。为了弥补这部分不足，我们同时提供了关于美国通用会计准则金额和非美国通用会计准则差别的具体信息。在后文的附表里列示了美国通用会计准则和非美国通用会计准则调节的明细，可以直观地进行比较。
财务报告附注
本财务报告中的财务信息（不包括非美国通用会计准则财务信息）是从按照美国通用会计准则准备的未经审计的搜狐公司财务报表中摘录的。
2006年6月20日
起，搜狐公司终止运营其电子商务平台，并将相关业务视为终止经营业务。为了使读者更关注持续经营业务，并保持财务数据的一致性，搜狐公司本期和以前期间的损益表中将单独披露终止经营业务。
在
2007年4月1日
以前报告期间内，游戏部门的大部分成本和费用都是为产品开发而发生。相应地，公司将所有发生的费用纪录在产品研发费用当中。自
2007年4月1日
开始，为了更好地反映运营绩效以进一步加强与同业的可比性，搜狐对与游戏运营相关的费用进行了重分类调整，主要是将游戏运营人员的薪酬福利费用从产品开发费用重分类至在线游戏业务的成本中。相应地，为保持与当前报告期间一致，公司也对以前报告期间公布的相关数据进行了重分类调整。上述重分类在2006年第三季度的金额为29.6万美元，在2006年前三个季度的金额为93.8万美元。
有关前瞻性陈述的警告声明
本财务报告中包含前瞻性的陈述。我们现在预计“业务展望”中的内容在下个季度财务报告公布之前不会被更新。但是，搜狐公司保留在任何时候，由于任何原因对“业务展望”部分的内容进行更新的权利。
非历史事实的陈述，包括关于我们的信念及预期，均为前瞻性陈述。这些陈述是基于当前的计划，估计及展望，请不要对其产生不适当的依赖。前瞻性的陈述中包含风险及不确定因素。我们在此提醒您，某些重要的因素可能会导致实际结果与前瞻性陈述有重大差别。潜在的风险及不确定因素包括但不限于：中华人民共和国产业政策的不确定、各季度运营结果可能出现上下波动、搜狐公司过去及未来可能的亏损、有限的营业历史、以及本公司仰赖在线广告销售、在线游戏和无线业务（其收入主要通过数家移动电信运营商取得）作为主要收入来源的事实。更多有关上述及其他风险的资讯收录于截至
2006年12月31日
的搜狐公司年报和10-K表格，以及向美国证券交易委员会提交的其他文件中。

(NASDAQ: SOHU)是中国领先的互联网品牌，是中国人生活中不可缺少的一部分，搜狐的网络资产以及基于web2.0产品的社区给众多的SOHU用户在信息、娱乐、交流、商务领域提供了非常广泛的选择。SOHU建立了中国最全面的互联网资产组合之一和自有搜索引擎，其中包括最大的门户和中国领先的互联网媒体网站

搜狐动态
2007
搜狐携手PremierGoals构建英超中文官网矩阵群
搜狐公司联席总裁兼首席财务官余楚媛、超级足球公司首席执行官亨里克-巴克、埃里克森、孙继海共同启动战略合作仪式
2007年11月13日，上海迎来了中国3000万英超球迷的盛事。北京2008年奥运会互联网内容服务赞助商搜狐公司和PremierGoals（超级足球公司）正式启动战略合作。超级足球公司引进英超包括利物浦、曼城、纽卡斯尔、托特纳姆热刺、布莱克本、埃弗顿、朴茨茅斯、阿斯顿维拉、伯明翰、博尔顿、德比郡、米德尔斯堡、雷丁、西汉姆、维冈竞技、富勒姆16家俱乐部的官方网站授权，由搜狐独家承建这些俱乐部的中文官网，构建了中国最大英超中文官网矩阵群(登录http://www.premiergoals.com )。
搜狐体育在与超级足球公司战略合作后，独家承建与推广英超中文官网矩阵，广大的球迷进入搜狐体育，将直接收看到16支英超豪强中文官网上最权威、最专业、最全面的英超赛事资讯和精彩进球视频。在国际市场拥有极高的市场认知度的超级足球公司，是俱乐部和足球协会的优质合作伙伴，凭借其全面的足球知识以及新媒体的全球经验，获得了英超16家俱乐部互联网和无线官方内容在中国的传播权利。
英超中文官网矩阵是中国唯一能提供免费延时收看英超16家俱乐部完整的全程赛事视频的传播渠道。通过新闻、图片、赛程、赛果、技术统计、积分榜、射手榜、球队介绍等8大版块，英超16支豪强第一次在中国网民面前集体亮相，全方位展现英超的魅力。各大俱乐部将为中文官网提供权威的官方内容，还独家提供各球队教练和球星们的幕后图片。此外，各俱乐部更提供了精彩的官方视频，不仅有球队的比赛集锦，球队征战欧冠等杯赛视频，更包括各大俱乐部球星访谈，与球迷进行最直接的交流互动。这些都是普通英超转播所没有的独家资源。
此次合作中最让中国英超球迷兴奋的是，通过与16家俱乐部的合作关系，搜狐体育播报将免费奉献英超07-08、08-09和09-10连续3个赛季的视频盛宴。从2007年8月11日至2008年5月11日进行的英超07-08赛季中，搜狐体育全程覆盖38轮380场精彩赛事，网络独家免费延时播放374场巅峰对决，让无法收看到英超直播的球迷通过搜狐体育观看到每一场比赛，各大赛事视频集锦、球星视频集锦等更是精彩纷呈。
超级足球首席执行官及合伙创办人亨里克-巴克、
搜狐公司联席总裁兼首席财务官余楚媛、搜狐公司体育中心总监兼北京2008奥运官方网站总编辑敖铭等出席了新闻发布会。
作为16家俱乐部的代表，曼城俱乐部主教练埃里克森和中国球员孙继海专程前来上海出席新闻发布会，引发媒体追逐热潮。当日，埃里克森和孙继海的博客正式落户搜狐独家承建的曼城俱乐部中文官网，这是第一批在中文官网上开博的英超球员和教练。自此，搜狐英超中文官网矩阵还将汇聚更多英超球星和教练的博客，中国英超球迷将便捷的通过博客与孙继海、埃里克森等英超球星进行零距离的交流互动。
曼城俱乐部主教练埃里克森表示，“能够把丰富的曼城官方网站的信息用中文传达，将帮助中国的曼城球迷更加贴近他们喜欢的球队和球星。很期待与广大中国球迷通过博客的方式进行交流”
超级足球首席执行官亨里克-巴克说,
“超级足球公司在国际足球界拥有独特的人脉。希望通过我们在业界的知名度，在新媒体传播方面的经验，以及对中国市场的熟悉，能给热情的中国球迷带来又好又多的国际足球的内容和激情。我们感觉非常荣幸能够和搜狐合作，
我们了解到从2006年世界杯开始，中国的网民已开始习惯上搜狐看视频的直播。我们希望通过我们和搜狐的合作能够更好地树立英国俱乐部在中国的品牌。”
搜狐公司联席总裁兼首席财务官余楚媛表示：“搜狐将凭借自身的优势，运用在网站运营的经验，以及对足球运动的深刻理解，为关注英超乃至世界足球的球迷们提供线上线下全方位服务。最有效的将英超的影响深入到中国球迷当中。希望搜狐体育能够成为广大网民与英超各大俱乐部之间的桥梁，让全球华人英超球迷也可以和世界各国使用英语的球迷一样，拥有真正属于自己的网上球迷乐园。”
此外，为了将英超16家俱乐部官网矩阵群打造成球迷狂欢的网络家园，搜狐体育还成立了16家俱乐部“最官方”的英超球迷联盟，为中国英超球迷搜罗独家新闻、比赛数据、球星档案、明星自传、花絮、官方论坛、球迷聚会，英超Fans的聚点等等，通过网友评选最佳阵容、撰写以英超为主题的博客征文，以及各种竞猜活动，让球迷们共同分享网上的激情英超。参加活动的球迷，不仅有机会获得球星签名球衣、足球、战靴、各球队原版纪念品以及队服等顶级珍藏品，更独享亲赴英伦主场看球，为喜爱的球星加油的尊贵特权。

搜狐中门户网站第一标
2008搜狐奥运将亮相央视
11月18日，搜狐亮相央视“2008中国有我”黄金时段广告招标会进行投标，并一举中标最火爆的新闻联播和天气预报之间7.5秒标版，拉开了2008年搜狐的强势奥运品牌推广的序幕，搜狐的奥运战略也由此进入一个新的阶段。这是互联网行业尤其是门户网站首次在央视黄金时段广告招标中亮相。这也是搜狐的奥运战略在完成资源和内容的领先之后，在营销和推广方面又开始的新一轮领跑。
每年一度央视黄金时段招标，被誉为“中国经济的晴雨表”和“品牌奥运会”，至今已经成功举办了13届。因央视黄金时段在中国的影响力和覆盖面，招标会成了品牌竞争的首要阵地，每次招标会吸引了全球各知名品牌和新锐品牌的积极关注和参与，每年通过中标央视黄金时段广告而在竞争中脱颖而出的企业数不胜数。
搜狐是北京2008奥运会唯一的互联网赞助商，随着奥运的日益临近，搜狐的奥运战略和品牌推广已经进入全面实施阶段。参加央视黄金资源广告招标，是搜狐2008奥运品牌策略的第一步，之后，搜狐将利用多种媒体渠道全面开展搜狐奥运传播，并举行形式多样的奥运互动活动，网民将有机会分享到包括门票、款待等多种优势的奥运资源。据透露，搜狐全新的奥运广告形象已经成形，网民将在2008年CCTV黄金段看到搜狐的全新奥运广告形象。
同时，选择参加央视黄金资源招标，不惜重金进行搜狐奥运品牌的推广，显示了搜狐对待奥运赞助商身份的严肃态度和推广的决心，搜狐董事局主席兼首席执行官张朝阳认为：“自从搜狐成为奥运赞助商，我们就一直在努力使搜狐成为网络奥运的冠军。搜狐参与CCTV招标，期待达到更多、更广泛的观众，在全国范围内，在全年龄段的观众中形成‘看奥运，上搜狐’的习惯。互联网已经和日化、医药、食品一样成为人们日常生活的一部分，我们终于可以凭借CCTV这样的大众的权威的媒体平台来进行推广。”
作为中国最大的门户网站和中国第一互联网品牌，搜狐在成为百年奥林匹克历史上第一个互联网赞助商之后，又成为第一个夺取央视黄金广告资源的互联网企业。借助央视的平台，搜狐将“奥运第一门户”的形象，以及独家奥运的资源和领先的奥运内容全面向14亿电视观众进行高效展示，使自己独家拥有了一个向最大的受众群体推荐自己的机会，以获得更多来自于电视的新用户，大规模提高搜狐网站流量，继续扩大自己在网络奥运大战中的优势，给广告客户更多的回报。
这也是北京2008年奥运会独家互联网赞助商同中国大陆独家播出机构的第二次握手。7月17日，搜狐同央视国际结成战略合作伙伴关系，双方全面共享、整合资源和用户，用户在搜狐网上即可欣赏到央视的精彩内容。通过与央视的战略合作，搜狐为用户提供了全新的网络收视体验。搜狐此次进行央视黄金时段的广告投标，更加紧密了同央视的合作，双方在奥运报道方面的联动也将进一步加强，搜狐也向建设百年老店的梦想更进了一步。
2008年是奥运年，奥运带来的商机将会对各个行业产生深远的影响，甚至会重构行业格局，在中国市场更是如此。作为奥运赞助商的搜狐，在巩固自己在奥运资源和奥运报道优势的同时，积极抢占奥运和品牌营销的制高点，强势出击最广泛的用户群体，凸显搜狐决战竞争对手的决心和信心，也为搜狐在竞争中取得完胜创造了条件。业内人士认为，搜狐此举，进一步加大了奥运营销中“强者恒强”的马太效应，为奥运营销建立了一个难以超越的竞争壁垒。
2007年以来，搜狐已经进入全面爆发的高速发展轨道，网站流量、网站粘性等有了大幅度的提高。此前发布的三季度财报显示，搜狐的增长速度明显高于竞争对手，同时，由于奥运资源和奥运内容的绝对领先，搜狐也是企业进行奥运网络营销的首选网站。搜狐财报发布前后持续的逆势大涨，更显示了华尔街分析师对搜狐的前景更加看好。
随着互联网的高速发展，以及用户获取信息方式的转变和升级，互联网已经被越来越多的人当作获取信息的重要途径。目前，中国已经拥有1.62亿网民，而且仍旧以两位数的速度迅猛发展，一度是小众高端群体使用的互联网，如今已同食品、日化、医药一样成为人们日常生活的重要部分。奥运作为中国全民关注的盛事，不分地域，不分年龄段。因此，搜狐选择用户群体规模最大的电视平台进行奥运战略推广，是扩大影响力和用户规模的最佳方式。中央电视台和搜狐之间的联动，将会大幅度地提高搜狐的用户数量和浏览量，为最大规模的网络用户群提供优质的网络体验。
